### [1] [AEVAL: From Anecdotal to Deterministic Testing for Agentic Skill Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16345)
*Tejas Singh Anand,Yuet Ying Christina Wang,Wanting Jiang,Steve Masson,Tian Zheng,Bingjie Zhou*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: AEVAL是一个集成到CI中的智能体技能评估框架，通过执行器与评分器分离、基于合约的测试和修复建议方案，实现了确定性、可重复的评估，避免自我纠正偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体技能评估依赖主观演示，缺乏可重复性和可比性，且无法在技能仓库中扩展，一次变更可能破坏多个工作流程。

Method: 提出AEVAL框架，采用变更触发的测试协议，每个技能需声明评估合约，在自动执行器中运行，并分离执行器和评分器，防止自我纠正偏差；评分使用首次尝试规则，并跟踪自我纠正；修复建议分为因果级和质量级。

Result: 在多个智能体SDK的生产环境中测试，AEVAL将虚假的100%通过率转化为可重复的首次尝试失败信号，并记录每次执行器修复。

Conclusion: AEVAL提供了一种可靠的智能体技能质量评估方法，将主观评估转变为基于证据的自动化CI流程。

中文摘要：现代智能体系统越来越依赖于技能：即包含自然语言和代码的可安装包，用于教会LLM智能体执行领域任务。随着技能库的增长，开发者需要每次变更的自动化质量信号，然而目前的评估很大程度上是传闻式的：开发者要求智能体“尝试该技能”，观看演示，然后形成主观印象。这既无法保证跨运行的可重复性，也无法保证跨版本的可比性，并且在市场环境中扩展性差，因为一次回归就能静默破坏数十个下游工作流程。我们提出了AEVAL（智能体评估），一个集成CI的框架，用确定性、可重复的测试流水线取代这种实践，用于评估智能体技能。每次技能变更都会触发一个测试事件：技能在自动执行器中运行，针对开发者声明的评估合约（eval.config），产生结构化的、基于证据的质量信号，下游CI可以据此进行路由。一个关键因素是执行器和评分器之间的结构分离，防止一种微妙但普遍的失败模式：智能体在执行过程中静默地自我纠正，然后对自己修补后的输出进行评分并判定为通过。我们的贡献是：（i）一种确定性的、变更触发的评估协议，包含每个技能的合约和每次运行的人工制品模式；（ii）将自我纠正偏差形式化为朴素智能体评估器的一种独特失败模式；（iii）执行器/评分器分离，带有首次尝试评分规则和明确的自我纠正跟踪；（iv）一个分层的、基于证据的修复建议方案（LV1因果，LV2质量），以内联合并请求注释的形式发布。在多个智能体SDK的生产级智能体栈中对真实技能进行验证，AEVAL将虚假的100%通过率转化为可重复的首次尝试失败信号，并附带每次执行器修复的可审计记录。

Original abstract: Modern agentic systems increasingly rely on skills: installable packages of natural language and code that teach an LLM agent to perform a domain task. As skill repositories grow, developers need automated quality signals on every change, yet evaluation today is largely anecdotal: a developer asks an agent to "try the skill," watches a demo, and forms a subjective impression. This yields neither reproducibility across runs nor comparability across versions, and scales poorly to marketplaces where one regression can silently break dozens of downstream workflows.
  We present AEVAL (Agentic Evaluation), a CI-integrated framework that replaces this practice with a deterministic, reproducible test pipeline for agentic skills. Every skill change triggers a test event: the skill runs against a developer-declared evaluation contract (eval.config) inside an automated executor, emitting a structured, evidence-grounded quality signal that downstream CI can route on.
  A key ingredient is a structural separation between executor and grader, preventing a subtle but pervasive failure mode: an agent that silently self-corrects during execution and then grades its own patched outputs as passing.
  Our contributions are: (i) a deterministic, change-triggered evaluation protocol with per-skill contracts and per-run artifact schemas; (ii) a formalization of self-correction bias as a distinct failure mode of naive agentic evaluators; (iii) an executor/grader separation with a first-attempt grading rule and explicit self-correction tracking; and (iv) a tiered, grounded-evidence fix-suggestion scheme (LV1 causal, LV2 quality) posted as inline merge-request comments. Validated on real skills in a production agentic stack across multiple agent SDKs, AEVAL converts spurious 100% pass rates into reproducible first-attempt fail signals with an auditable record of every executor fix.

</details>


### [2] [AoA: Theorem Proving Agent over Abstract Syntax Tree of Redesigned Language](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16372)
*Qiyuan Xu,Joshua Ong Jun Leang,Renxi Wang,Wenda Li,Haonan Li,Luke Ong,Conrad Watt*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出Agent over AST (AoA)，通过将证明代理从具体语法提升到抽象语法树，显著降低LLM-based proof agents的令牌消耗和API成本，并支持新语言Minilang。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于LLM的证明代理因操作具体语法导致高令牌消耗和API成本，且新语言Minilang因未被训练语料覆盖而难以采用。

Method: 将代理从源代码提升到抽象语法树：模型以JSON形式提供Minilang的AST证明，通过树编辑模型融合证明操作和状态。

Result: 在miniF2F和NTP4VC-Pearl上，相比Amazon Isabelle Agent，API成本降低2.3-4.7倍，令牌使用减少2.9-6.9倍，工具调用减少3.9-8.9倍，速度提升1.4-2.0倍，并在更难基准上解决更多问题。

Conclusion: AoA有效降低了成本并提升了性能，同时解决了新语言Minilang的采用问题。

中文摘要：交互式定理证明（ITP）支撑着程序验证和形式化数学，但其手动工作限制了可扩展性。基于LLM的证明代理有望减轻这一工作，但其大量的令牌消耗和API成本仍然是一个主要障碍。我们将这一成本追溯到一个共同的根源：当前的代理操作基于序列化的具体语法，以源代码文本形式输出证明，并通过基于行号的独立查询恢复证明状态，因此每次编辑都会改变后续行，并迫使错误和状态反复重新定位。这种对具体语法的依赖也阻碍了Minilang的采用，Minilang是一种最新的证明语言，在基于LLM的证明中达到了SOTA，但对于LLM的训练语料库来说太新了。我们通过将代理从源代码提升到抽象语法树（AST）来解决这两个问题：模型以Minilang的AST的JSON表示形式提供证明——这对于工具调用型LLM来说是原生的——并通过树编辑模型驱动证明器，该模型将证明操作和状态融合到一个证明树中，因此每个操作都携带自己的子目标状态，可以直接从树中读取。我们在Agent over AST (AoA)中实现了这一设计。与Amazon的Isabelle Agent在miniF2F和NTP4VC-Pearl公共成功集上相比，AoA将API成本降低了2.3-4.7倍（归一化输入缓存记账），使用了2.9-6.9倍更少的令牌和3.9-8.9倍更少的工具调用，完成速度提高了1.4-2.0倍——同时在更难的验证基准上解决了更多问题。

Original abstract: Interactive theorem proving (ITP) underpins program verification and formalized mathematics, but its manual effort limits scalability. LLM-based proof agents promise to ease this effort, but their heavy token consumption and API cost remain a major obstacle. We trace this cost to a shared root: current agents operate on serialized concrete syntax, emitting proofs as source text and recovering proof states through separate, line-number-based queries, so every edit shifts later lines and forces repeated relocation of errors and states. This same dependence on concrete syntax also blocks adoption of Minilang, a recent proof language that reaches SOTA on LLM-based proving but is too new for LLMs' training corpora. We address both problems by lifting the agent off source text and onto the abstract syntax tree (AST): the model supplies proofs as JSON representations of Minilang's AST -- native to tool-calling LLMs -- and drives the prover through a tree-edit model that fuses proof operations and states into one proof tree, so each operation carries its own subgoal's state, readable directly off the tree. We realize this design in \emph{Agent over AST} (AoA). Against Amazon's Isabelle Agent on miniF2F and NTP4VC-Pearl common success sets, AoA cuts API cost by 2.3--4.7x (normalized input-cache accounting), uses 2.9--6.9x fewer tokens and 3.9--8.9x fewer tool calls, and finishes 1.4--2.0x faster -- while also solving far more problems on the harder verification benchmark.

</details>


### [3] [Fantastic Adaptive Taxonomies and How to Use Them](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16387)
*Mert Cemri,Andrei Cojocaru,Melissa Pan,Shu Liu,Shubham Agarwal,Alexander Krentsel,Jay Tang,Kannan Ramchandran,Joseph E. Gonzalez,Matei Zaharia,Alex Dimakis,Ion Stoica*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出AdaMAST，通过将智能体执行轨迹自动归纳为紧凑的失败分类法（沿三个固定轴），作为共享反馈接口，在搜索、运行时和轨迹选择中显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原始轨迹作为反馈媒介存在冗长、实例特定和缺乏稳定词汇的问题，难以有效积累和重用失败信息。

Method: AdaMAST将目标系统轨迹转换为沿系统级、角色特定和领域特定三个固定轴组织的命名失败代码分类法，所有名称、定义和证据模式均从轨迹中自动归纳。

Result: 在搜索、运行时和轨迹选择三个场景中均取得显著提升：搜索优于自由反思，SWE-agent解决率从60%升至70%，Claude Code从64.0%升至70.7%，轨迹选择准确率提升8-15个百分点。

Conclusion: 自适应失败分类法有效闭环了轨迹与改进程序之间的循环，具有紧凑性、人类忠实性和适应性优势。

中文摘要：一个智能体系统的执行轨迹记录了它如何失败，而改进此类系统而不改变模型权重的程序（轨迹选择、提示和工作流优化、运行时监控）会读取这些轨迹以获取反馈。然而，原始轨迹是积累这种反馈的糟糕媒介：冗长、实例特定，并且缺乏描述重复失败的稳定词汇。我们认为，智能体系统应该维护一个明确表示其如何失败的表示，该表示从其自身行为中归纳得出，并且可以在需要失败反馈的任何地方重复使用。AdaMAST通过将目标系统的轨迹转换为紧凑的、基于证据的失败分类法来构建这种表示：沿着三个固定轴（系统级、角色特定和领域特定）组织的命名失败代码，每个名称、定义和证据模式都是从轨迹中归纳得出的；没有手工编写的代码，也没有人工注释的轨迹。这种分类法不仅仅是事后诊断，而是一个共享的反馈接口，以三种方式改进智能体。在智能体系统搜索中，基于分类法编码的失败候选诊断在所有五个测试基准上都优于自由形式的反思。在运行时，分类法反馈将SWE-agent在SWE-bench Verified Mini上的解决率从60%（使用自由文本反思）提高到70%，并将Claude Code作为运行时技能从64.0%提高到70.7%。在轨迹选择中，基于归纳代码构建的验证器AdaMAST-Judge在Terminal-Bench 2.0上将最佳-of-5准确率比Pass@1提高了8-15个百分点。该词汇本身是紧凑的（一个数量级的压缩，同时保留轨迹区分性）、符合人类判断的（比手工编写的参考词汇更接近专家失败注释）并且适应性强（为不同领域归纳的分类法共享很少的代码）。自适应失败分类法闭环了智能体生成的轨迹与改进它们的程序之间的循环。

Original abstract: An agent system's execution traces record how it fails, and procedures that improve such a system without changing model weights (trajectory selection, prompt and workflow optimization, runtime monitoring) read these traces for feedback. Yet raw traces are a poor medium for accumulating that feedback: long, instance-specific, and lacking a stable vocabulary for recurring failures. We argue that an agent system should instead maintain an explicit representation of how it fails, induced from its own behavior and reusable wherever failure feedback is needed. AdaMAST builds this representation by converting a target system's traces into a compact, evidence-grounded failure taxonomy: named failure codes organized along three fixed axes (system-level, role-specific, and domain-specific), with every name, definition, and evidence pattern induced from the traces; no code is hand-authored, no trace human-annotated. The taxonomy is not merely a post-hoc diagnostic but a shared feedback interface, improving agents in three ways. In agent-system search, taxonomy-coded diagnoses of failed candidates outperform free-form reflection on all five benchmarks we test. At runtime, taxonomy feedback raises SWE-agent's resolution on SWE-bench Verified Mini from 60% with free-text reflection to 70%, and improves Claude Code from 64.0% to 70.7% as a runtime skill. In trajectory selection, AdaMAST-Judge, a verifier built on the induced codes, improves best-of-5 accuracy on Terminal-Bench 2.0 by 8-15 points over Pass@1. The vocabulary itself is compact (an order-of-magnitude compression that preserves trace distinctions), human-faithful (matching expert failure annotations more closely than a hand-crafted reference vocabulary), and adaptive (taxonomies induced for different domains share few codes). Adaptive failure taxonomies close the loop between the traces agents produce and the procedures that improve them.

</details>


### [4] [When to Use Which? Benchmarking Optimisers for Configurable Systems under Varying Budgets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16476)
*Chao Jiang,Yulong Ye,Tao Chen,Miqing Li*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 比较了不同预算下多种优化器的性能，发现FLASH优化器在各种预算下表现稳定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 用户面临不同预算，需要知道在给定预算下哪个优化器最佳。

Method: 系统评估8种优化器在22个系统上不同预算水平的表现。

Result: 基于模型的优化器在紧预算下好，无模型在宽松预算下好，但FLASH始终表现好。

Conclusion: 许多系统有好的局部最优，贪婪优化器如FLASH因此有效。

中文摘要：软件配置调优对于优化系统性能至关重要，过去十年中出现了各种优化器。然而，调优过程中所需的时间可能因系统而异。在某些系统（例如PostgreSQL）中，测量一个配置可能需要几分钟，而在其他系统（例如MariaDB）中，可能需要几个小时。此外，即使在同一系统中，用户可能有不同的预算和偏好设置。这自然引出了一个问题——在给定的预算水平下，哪个优化器是软件工程从业者的最佳选择？这很重要，因为优化器通常有自己的“舒适区”，并且在不同的预算下表现可能非常不同。在本文中，我们旨在回答这个问题。我们系统地评估了八种成熟的优化器在22个可配置系统上不同预算水平下的表现。我们发现，不出所料，基于模型的优化器（例如SMAC）在预算紧张时表现良好，而无需模型的优化器（例如遗传算法）在预算充足时表现更优。然而，有趣的是，有一种优化器FLASH在大多数系统上无论预算多少都表现一致良好。最后，我们研究了这种现象的原因，发现许多系统拥有良好的局部最优（具有大的吸引域），使得贪婪优化器（例如FLASH）能够实现强性能。本工作的源代码、数据和补充材料可在https://anonymous.4open.science/r/Config-W2W-98B2获取。

Original abstract: Software configuration tuning is crucial for optimising system performance, and various optimisers have emerged over the last decade. Yet, the time required during the tuning process may vary across systems. In some systems (e.g., PostgreSQL), it may take a few minutes to measure a configuration, whereas in some others (e.g., MariaDB), it can take several hours. Moreover, even within the same system, users may have varying budgets and preferred settings. This naturally raises a question -- Given a budget level, which optimiser is the best choice for SE practitioners? This matters because optimisers usually have their own ``comfort zone'' and may perform very differently under distinct budgets.
  In this paper, we aim to answer this question. We systematically evaluate eight well-established optimisers across 22 configurable systems under varying budget levels. We find that, unsurprisingly, model-based optimisers (e.g., SMAC) are well-suited under tight budgets, and model-free optimisers (e.g., GAs) become superior with more generous budgets. However, interestingly, there is one optimiser, FLASH, that performs consistently well on most systems regardless of budgets. We lastly investigate the reasons behind this phenomenon and find that many systems possess good local optima (with large basins of attraction), allowing greedy optimisers (e.g., FLASH) to achieve strong performance.
  Source code, data, and supplementary materials of this work are available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/Config-W2W-98B2.

</details>


### [5] [Personalized Assessments from Personal Artifacts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16494)
*Yufan Zhang,Jaromir Savelka,Seth Copen Goldstein,Majd Sakr*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了一种自动生成的个性化探测谜题方法，用于评估学生对自身代码的理解，实验表明能识别理解差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI编码代理导致学生和专业人士可能不理解自己的代码，威胁学术诚信和专业责任，需要评估代码理解的方法。

Method: 开发了Personalized Probing Puzzles ($p^3$)，自动生成谜题，异步管理，快速完成。

Result: 在研究生云课程中测试，初步表明能帮助识别学生对自身代码理解的潜在差距。

Conclusion: 未来需将谜题结果与代码理解关联，并嵌入专业代码审查过程。

中文摘要：人工智能驱动的编码代理的快速发展和普及意味着软件工程学生和专业人士不能被视为理解他们自己的代码，这危及了学术诚信和专业责任。我们开发了一种称为个性化探测谜题（$p^3$）的方法来评估学生对自己代码的理解，并在研究生级别的云计算课程中测试了$p^3$。我们的初步研究表明，$p^3$可以帮助识别学生对自己代码理解方面的潜在差距。这些谜题是自动生成的，异步管理的，并在几分钟内完成。未来的工作需要将谜题结果与代码理解相关联，并将$p^3$嵌入到专业的代码审查过程中。

Original abstract: The rapid development and popularization of AI-enabled coding agents have meant software engineering students and professionals cannot be assumed to understand their own code, which risks academic integrity and professional accountability. We developed a method called Personalized Probing Puzzles ($p^3$) to evaluate students' understanding of their own code, and tested $p^3$ in a graduate-level cloud computing course. Our pilot study shows that $p^3$ can help identify potential gaps in students' understanding of their own code. The puzzles are automatically generated, asynchronously administered, and finished in minutes. Future work is needed to correlate puzzle results with code understanding and to embed $p^3$ in a professional code review process.

</details>


### [6] [ReqGenX: An Empirical Study of Atomic Decomposition, Artifact Regeneration, and Reconstruction for Legacy SRS Documents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16564)
*Ragib Shahariar Ayon,Rayed Fahmi,Sumon Biswas,Shibbir Ahmed*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出ReqGenX管道将传统SRS文档转化为可追溯的合成预SRS工件，以支持LLM生成SRS的细粒度评估，实验表明该方法在忠实性、质量和信息保留方面表现良好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据集缺乏源需求、中间工件和生成规格之间的细粒度可追溯性，难以评估基于LLM的SRS生成。

Method: 设计ReqGenX管道：将SRS分解为原子语句，通过多LLM投票分类为不同工件类型，并用约束提示和法官指导精炼生成工件。

Result: 原子忠实性高（AlignScore中位数0.96-0.99），生成工件与源原子强对齐（AlignScore 0.80-0.94，法官通过率近100%），下游重构中原子可恢复（SBERT均值0.69-0.75）。

Conclusion: 合成预SRS工件支持细粒度评估，但存在忠实性、信息保留和完整性之间的权衡。

中文摘要：背景：评估自动化软件需求规格说明（SRS）生成具有挑战性，因为很少有数据集提供源需求、中间获取工件和生成规格说明之间的细粒度可追溯性。目标：我们旨在研究是否可以将传统SRS文档转换为可追溯的合成预SRS工件，以支持基于LLM的SRS生成的细粒度评估。方法：我们使用ReqGenX进行了一项实证研究，这是一个受控管道，它将SRS部分分解为基于源的原子语句，通过多LLM多数投票将原子路由到标准启发的工件类型，并使用约束提示和迭代法官引导的精炼生成工件。我们在七份纯SRS文档上评估了ReqGenX，使用基础性、质量、信息保留和下游重构分析。结果：ReqGenX生成忠实且可用的原子，AlignScore中位数通常在0.96到0.99之间，Prometheus得分在4.34到4.85之间。生成的工件仍然强基于它们的源原子，AlignScore值通常在0.80到0.94之间，法官通过率接近100%；更严格的Prometheus评估产生的通过率在54.8%到97.1%之间。在下游SRS重构案例研究中，基于工件的原子从生成的SRS中仍然可恢复，SBERT均值在0.69到0.75之间，AlignScore中位数在0.76到0.84之间。结论：可追溯的合成预SRS工件可以支持更细粒度的基于LLM的SRS生成评估，同时暴露了忠实性、信息保留和工件完整性之间的权衡。

Original abstract: Background: Evaluating automated Software Requirements Specification (SRS) generation is challenging because few datasets provide fine-grained traceability between source requirements, intermediate elicitation artifacts, and generated specifications. Aims: We aim to study whether legacy SRS documents can be transformed into traceable synthetic pre-SRS artifacts that support fine-grained evaluation of LLM-based SRS generation. Method: We conduct an empirical study using ReqGenX, a controlled pipeline that decomposes SRS sections into source-grounded atomic statements, routes atoms to standards-inspired artifact types through multi-LLM plurality voting, and generates artifacts using constrained prompts with iterative judge-guided refinement. We evaluate ReqGenX on seven PURE SRS documents using grounding, quality, information retention, and downstream reconstruction analyses. Results: ReqGenX produces faithful and usable atoms, with median AlignScore values typically between 0.96 and 0.99 and Prometheus scores ranging from 4.34 to 4.85. Generated artifacts remain strongly grounded in their source atoms, with AlignScore values typically between 0.80--0.94 and judge pass rates near 100%; stricter Prometheus evaluation yields pass rates from 54.8% to 97.1%. In a downstream SRS reconstruction case study, artifact-backed atoms remain recoverable from generated SRSs, with SBERT means between 0.69 and 0.75 and AlignScore medians between 0.76 and 0.84. Conclusions: Traceable synthetic pre-SRS artifacts can support more fine-grained evaluation of LLM-based SRS generation, while exposing tradeoffs among faithfulness, information retention, and artifact completeness.

### [7] [From Discussion to Execution: Replicating Buggy and Correct Data Science Code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16569)
*Ragib Shahariar Ayon,Mohammad Wardat,Shibbir Ahmed*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了Reprodgen框架，利用LLM从Q&A帖子自动复现可执行的错误/修复代码对，通过结构化的代码意图和思维链迭代优化，在多个数据科学库上验证了有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从非正式Q&A论坛复现可靠数据科学代码困难，因为信息不完整且非结构化，限制自动化调试与验证。

Method: 提出Reprodgen框架，构建代码意图（CI）、功能需求（FR）和结构化思维链（SCoT）表示，利用LLM迭代优化代码直到可执行且语义一致。

Result: 在Stack Overflow和GitHub Issues上对七个库评估，构建了可运行代码基准，显示可靠复现且模型性能差异明显。

Conclusion: Reprodgen能有效从Q&A帖子复现可执行的错误和修复代码，为自动化调试提供支持。

中文摘要：从非正式来源复现可靠的数据科学代码具有挑战性，原因包括模糊的问题规范、缺失的依赖项和性能瓶颈。尽管开发者Q&A论坛提供了关于诊断和修复实际问题的丰富讨论，但信息往往不完整且非结构化，限制了其在自动调试和验证中的应用。在本文中，我们介绍了Reprodgen，一个基于大型语言模型（LLM）的框架，用于从Q&A论坛帖子中自动复现可执行的错误和修复后的数据科学程序。给定一个问题及其对应的答案，Reprodgen重构问题中描述的错误行为和答案中描述的预期修复，生成反映原始讨论的可执行错误和修复代码对。该框架构建代码意图（CI）、功能需求（FR）和结构化思维链（SCoT）的结构化表示，并使用基于LLM的审核器迭代优化代码，直到其可执行且语义一致。我们在Stack Overflow（SO）和GitHub Issues（GI）上对七个数据科学库（包括pandas、numpy和scikit-learn）评估了Reprodgen，并构建了一个由人类专家验证的可运行错误和修复程序基准。我们的流程使用LLM进行语义评估，而可执行性通过实际执行验证。结果显示可靠的复现，且模型性能存在明显差异。

Original abstract: Reproducing reliable data science code from informal sources is challenging due to ambiguous problem specifications, missing dependencies, and performance bottlenecks. Although developer Q&A forums provide rich discussions on diagnosing and fixing real-world issues, the information is often incomplete and unstructured, limiting its use for automated debugging and verification. In this paper, we introduce Reprodgen, a large language model (LLM) based framework for automatically replicating executable buggy and patched data science programs from Q&A forum posts. Given a question and its corresponding answer, Reprodgen reconstructs the buggy behavior described in the question and the intended fix described in the answer, producing executable buggy and patched code pairs that reflect the original discussion. The framework builds structured representations of code intent (CI), functional requirements (FR), and Structured Chain of Thought (SCoT), and iteratively refines code using an LLM-based reviewer until it is executable and semantically consistent. We evaluate Reprodgen on Stack Overflow (SO) and GitHub Issues (GI) across seven data science libraries, including pandas, numpy, and scikit-learn, and construct a benchmark of runnable buggy and patched programs validated by human experts. Our pipeline uses LLMs for semantic assessment, while executability is verified through actual execution. Results show reliable replication with clear differences in model performance.

### [8] [DataFlow-Harness: A Grounded Code-Agent Platform for Constructing Editable LLM Data Pipelines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16617)
*Runming He,Zhen Hao Wong,Hao Liang,Zimo Meng,Chengyu Shen,Xiaochen Ma,Wentao Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: DataFlow-Harness通过类型化增量变异指导LLM构建平台原生DAG，在12任务基准上达到93.3%通过率，相比Vanilla Claude Code成本降低72.5%、延迟降低49.9%，与上下文感知基线性能相当且成本低42.8%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有编码代理生成的脚本无法自动成为持久化、可编辑的平台工件，存在NL2Pipeline gap。

Method: 提出DataFlow-Harness平台，结合DataFlow-Skills（程序性指导）、MCP层（暴露算子注册表和管道状态）和DataFlow-WebUI（同步对话与可视化DAG编辑器），通过类型化增量变异构建DAG。

Result: 在12任务数据工程基准上，端到端通过率93.3%；与Vanilla Claude Code相比，成本降低72.5%，延迟降低49.9%；与Context-Aware Claude Code基线相比，通过率相差0.9个百分点，成本低42.8%。

Conclusion: 实时平台接地能产生持久、可编辑的工作流工件，其可靠性接近脚本生成基线，且构建成本和延迟更低。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地被用于自动化数据处理工作流，但编码代理通常生成的脚本不会自动作为持久化、可编辑的平台工件被实体化。我们将这种脱节称为NL2Pipeline鸿沟。为了弥合这一鸿沟，我们引入了DataFlow-Harness，一个指导LLM代理通过类型化的增量变异（而非自由格式脚本）来构建平台原生有向无环图（DAG）的平台。该平台结合了用于程序性指导的DataFlow-Skills、暴露实时算子注册表和当前管道状态的模型上下文协议（MCP）层，以及将对话式创作与可视化DAG编辑器同步的DataFlow-WebUI。在一个12任务的数据工程基准测试中，DataFlow-Harness实现了93.3%的观察端到端通过率。相对于Vanilla Claude Code，它减少了72.5%的测量货币成本和49.9%的生成延迟；其观察通过率与Context-Aware Claude Code基线相差0.9个百分点，而成本低42.8%。每任务分析表明，当构造依赖于隐式程序知识时，技能最为有用。这些结果表明，实时平台接地可以产生持久、可编辑的工作流工件，其观察可靠性接近脚本生成基线，并且具有更低的测量构建成本和延迟。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to automate data-processing workflows, yet coding agents typically produce scripts that are not automatically materialized as persistent, editable platform artifacts. We call this disconnect the \textit{NL2Pipeline gap}. To bridge it, we introduce \textsc{DataFlow-Harness}, a platform that guides an LLM agent to construct platform-native directed acyclic graphs (DAGs) through typed, incremental mutations rather than free-form scripts. The platform combines \textsc{DataFlow-Skills} for procedural guidance, a Model Context Protocol (MCP) layer that exposes the live operator registry and current pipeline state, and \textsc{DataFlow-WebUI}, which synchronizes conversational authoring with a visual DAG editor. On a 12-task data-engineering benchmark, \textsc{DataFlow-Harness} achieves a 93.3\% observed end-to-end pass rate. Relative to Vanilla Claude Code, it reduces measured monetary cost by 72.5\% and generation latency by 49.9\%; its observed pass rate is within 0.9 percentage points of the Context-Aware Claude Code baseline while its cost is 42.8\% lower. Per-task analysis indicates that Skills are most useful when construction depends on implicit procedural knowledge. These results show that live platform grounding can produce persistent, editable workflow artifacts with an observed reliability close to script-generation baselines and with lower measured construction cost and latency.

### [9] [CLOSER-Bench: Evaluating Budgeted Cross-Stage Design Closure for Hardware Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16632)
*Peilong Zhou,Zhirong Chen,Cangyuan Li,Haoyu Gao,Kaiyan Chang,Ziming Qu,Ying Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: CLOSER-Bench是一个硬件跨阶段设计收敛评估基准，揭示代理在完成-收敛上的差距，将硬件设计视为序列决策问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准难以评估代理在跨抽象边界的长周期硬件设计任务中的表现，缺乏统一的受控评估协议。

Method: 提出CLOSER-Bench，通过配对spec-to-RTL、RTL-to-GDS和spec-to-GDS任务，记录工具调用，测量质量、进展、成本和恢复能力。

Result: 试点实验显示代理在局部修复任务中成功，但在验证收敛任务中存在显著差距，且完整RTL-to-GDS流程验证了有效性。

Conclusion: 硬件收敛应被视为有预算约束的序列决策问题，而非独立代码生成任务。

中文摘要：硬件工程使编码代理面临一种难以通过pass-at-k捕获的长周期工作形式：进展是连续的，工具反馈是延迟且异构的，后端故障可能需要修改RTL而不是调整另一个物理设计参数。现有基准衡量RTL生成、仓库修复、验证、PPA演进或物理实现，但它们不同的设计和预言的差异使得难以确定代理在跨抽象边界时成功或失败的位置。我们引入了CLOSER-Bench，一种针对预算约束的跨阶段设计收敛的受控评估协议。对于一个设计和一个隐藏目标，它配对spec-to-RTL、RTL-to-GDS和spec-to-GDS任务，记录每次模拟器、综合、STA和布局布线调用，并测量最终质量、任何时候的进展、工具成本和跨阶段恢复。该基准构建于开源Verilator、Yosys、OpenROAD、KLayout、Sky130和Harbor代理框架之上。一个包含十个任务的试点项目，涵盖RTL修复、基于突变的验证、覆盖率、PPA优化、设计空间探索、跨模型调试和安全，建立了可执行的框架并揭示了尖锐的完成-收敛差距：三个代理解决了一个局部的AXI修复任务，而匹配的验证收敛任务将一个前沿代理与两个其他成功的基线区分开来。我们进一步验证了一个完整的RTL-to-GDS流程，并为阶段配对评估构建了一个基于宏的AXI/DMA流加速器。这些结果促使将硬件收敛视为一个有预算约束的序列决策问题，而非独立代码生成任务的集合。

Original abstract: Hardware engineering exposes coding agents to a form of long-horizon work that is difficult to capture with pass-at-k: progress is continuous, tool feedback is delayed and heterogeneous, and a backend failure may require revising RTL rather than tuning another physical-design parameter. Existing benchmarks measure RTL generation, repository repair, verification, PPA evolution, or physical implementation, but their different designs and oracles make it hard to determine where an agent succeeds or fails across abstraction boundaries. We introduce CLOSER-Bench, a controlled evaluation protocol for budgeted cross-stage design closure. For one design and one hidden objective, it pairs spec-to-RTL, RTL-to-GDS, and spec-to-GDS tasks, records every simulator, synthesis, STA, and place-and-route invocation, and measures final quality, anytime progress, tool cost, and cross-stage recovery. The benchmark is built on open-source Verilator, Yosys, OpenROAD, KLayout, Sky130, and the Harbor agent harness. A ten-task pilot spanning RTL repair, mutation-based verification, coverage, PPA optimization, design-space exploration, cross-model debugging, and security establishes the executable harness and exposes a sharp completion--closure gap: three agents solve a localized AXI repair task, while the matched verification-closure task separates a frontier agent from two otherwise successful baselines. We further validate a full RTL-to-GDS flow and construct a macro-based AXI/DMA streaming accelerator for the stage-paired evaluation. These results motivate treating hardware closure as a budgeted sequential decision problem rather than a collection of independent code generation tasks.

### [10] [Falsification-Based Verification of LLM-Generated Optimization Models: Sound Test Batteries and Their Detection Limits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16646)
*Haifeng Li,Mo Hai*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出基于证伪的验证框架，通过一系列可靠测试检测优化模型翻译中的错误，实现零假阳性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型将自然语言描述转化为优化模型时可能无声地失败，需要一种无需参考模型的验证方法。

Method: 基于证伪理论，从对偶性、比较静态分析和多面体极限推导方向、曲率等六类测试，仅通过求解器调用对槽位变换后的实例进行测试。

Result: 在326个模型上，假阳性率0.0%（对比阈值测试器54.9%），检测70.0%的条件类突变，并捕获40.4%执行准确性评分不可见的突变。

Conclusion: 该验证方法设计上保证零假阳性，能有效检测多种错误类别，实验证实了理论预测的可检测性模式。

中文摘要：大型语言模型现在能够将决策问题的自然语言描述转换为可直接求解的优化模型，但它们会无声地失败。生成的模型通常可以运行，但仍会构建错误的问题。本文针对这一场景开发了一种基于证伪的验证理论。描述中的每个数值量都是一个有类型的槽位，候选模型仅通过调用求解器对槽位变换后的实例进行测试，不参考任何参考模型或标签。从对偶性、比较静态分析和多面体极限论证中，我们推导出一系列测试类别，涵盖方向、曲率、挤压探测、禁止极限、湮灭和交换。每个测试都是可靠的，因此违反即证明不忠实，假阳性率在设计上为零。我们刻画了这种验证永远无法看到的内容，给出了在何种条件下可以确定检测到标准错误类别，并证明了没有固定阈值的扰动测试器能够同时做到可靠且非平凡。在来自NL4OPT和四个基准家族的326个真实模型上的实验证实了该理论。该测试集的假阳性率为0.0%，而阈值测试器为54.9%；它检测到了70.0%的已验证条件类突变，定罪了40.4%的执行准确性评分不可见的突变，并复现了预测的可检测性模式，包括其中的零点。

Original abstract: Large language models now translate natural-language descriptions of decision problems into solver-ready optimization models, but they fail silently. A generated model often runs and still formulates the wrong problem. This paper develops a theory of falsification-based verification for this setting. Every numeric quantity in the description is a typed slot, and a candidate model is tested only through solver calls on slot-transformed instances; no reference model or label is consulted. From duality, comparative statics, and polyhedral limit arguments we derive a battery of test classes covering directions, curvature, crush probes, prohibitive limits, annihilation, and exchange. Every test is sound, so a violation certifies unfaithfulness and the false-positive rate is zero by design. We characterize what such verification can never see, give conditions under which the canonical error classes are detected with certainty, and prove that no fixed-threshold perturbation tester is simultaneously sound and nontrivial. Experiments on 326 ground-truth models from NL4OPT and four benchmark families confirm the theory. The battery attains a 0.0% false-positive rate against 54.9% for a threshold tester, detects 70.0% of certified conditional-class mutants, convicts 40.4% of the mutants invisible to execution-accuracy scoring, and reproduces the predicted detectability pattern including its zeros.

</details>


### [11] [How Do You Choose Your AI Component? An Interview Study of Secure AI Integration in Practice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16660)
*Mahzabin Tamanna,Elizabeth Lin,Sparsha Gowda,Laurie Williams,Dominik Wermke*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 大型语言模型作为AI组件引入软件供应链时，从业者优先考虑功能而非安全，重复了传统软件依赖管理的错误；研究通过访谈22位从业者发现这一现象并提出安全设计建议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLMs作为AI组件在软件系统中的采用带来了新的安全风险，但缺乏指导如何安全选择与集成组件的知识；理解从业者的决策过程和安全考虑至关重要。

Method: 采用探索性半结构化访谈研究，对22名软件开发者、架构师和AI从业者进行访谈，分析其选择与集成AI组件时的决策标准和安全考虑。

Result: 模型选择主要由性能、准确性、成本和特定功能驱动，安全性极少被考虑；整个集成过程缺乏安全关注，行业正在重复传统软件依赖管理的历史错误。

Conclusion: 需要采取主动的安全设计方法，将安全评估纳入组件选择并在开发生命周期中持续，并为AI采用者、模型提供者和研究人员提出可操作建议。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）作为AI组件在现代软件系统中的日益普及，给软件供应链带来了独特的安全风险。尽管传统软件供应链的组件已有许多考虑和安全机制，但AI组件和平台的快速采用却忽视了这些来之不易的经验教训。在没有明确指导如何选择影响系统安全性的AI模型的情况下，选择并集成它们可能会使应用程序面临威胁，例如恶意组件、数据泄漏和意外行为。本研究的目的是通过一项探索性的半结构化访谈研究，了解从业者在选择与集成AI组件时的决策过程和安全考虑。为此，我们对来自不同组织的22名软件开发人员、架构师和AI从业者进行了半结构化访谈，内容涉及他们如何将AI组件集成到软件中。我们的分析发现，从业者的模型选择主要受功能标准驱动，包括性能、准确性、成本和特定功能（如工具调用或多模态支持），而安全性很少被作为评估标准。我们观察到在整个AI组件集成过程中始终缺乏安全关注，既有的软件供应链教训被忽视或忽略。该行业正在重复早期软件依赖管理中代价高昂的历史错误，优先考虑快速复用和可用性而非安全性和来源。我们将我们的发现提炼为对AI采用者、模型提供者和研究人员的可操作建议，倡导一种主动的、安全设计的方法，将安全评估整合到组件选择中，并在整个软件开发生命周期中持续进行。

Original abstract: The increasing adoption of Large Language Models (LLMs) as AI components in modern software systems introduces distinct security risks to the software supply chain. While many considerations and safety mechanisms are in place for components of the traditional software supply chain, the recent rapid adoption of AI components and platforms has overlooked these hard learned lessons. Selecting and integrating AI models without clear guidance on how these choices affect system security may leave applications vulnerable to threats, such as malicious components, data leakage, and unintended behavior. The goal of this study is to understand practitioners' decision making process and security considerations in selecting and integrating AI components through an exploratory semi-structured interview study. Toward this goal, we conducted semistructured interviews with 22 software developers, architects, and AI practitioners across diverse organizations about how they integrate AI components into their software.
  Our analysis finds that practitioners' model selection is predominantly driven by functional criteria, including performance, accuracy, cost, and specific features, e.g., tool calling or multimodal support, while security is rarely considered as an evaluation criterion. We observe a consistent lack of security concern throughout the AI component integration process, with established software supply chain lessons overlooked or ignored. The industry is repeating the historically costly mistakes of early software dependency management, prioritizing rapid reuse and availability over security and provenance. We distill our findings into actionable recommendations for AI adopters, model providers, and researchers, advocating for a proactive, security-by-design approach that integrates security evaluation into component selection and sustains it throughout the software development lifecycle.

</details>


### [12] [Specification-Driven Development as the Foundation of AI-Native Enterprise Software Engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16680)
*Mamdouh Alenezi*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文识别了无监管AI生成的失败模式，提出了规范治理参考模型（SGRM），并通过实证证明了其在减少安全缺陷和缩短上市时间方面的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决无监管对话式AI生成在软件工程中导致的失败模式，如生产力-可靠性悖论、架构侵蚀、安全暴露和技术债务。

Method: 基于文献语料库识别失败模式，提出SGRM框架（定义规范契约、确定性验证、三个严谨级别和闭环架构），并根据ISO/IEC 25010评估。

Result: 在宪法约束下安全缺陷减少73%，上市时间减少50%。

Conclusion: 氛围编码适用于构思和快速原型，但企业软件需要规范治理将概率生成转化为确定性工程。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）和代理型人工智能正在将软件工程从手动编码转向意图规范、架构和治理。出现了两种范式：氛围编码（vibe coding），一种直觉驱动的方法，通过观察行为接受AI产物；以及规范驱动开发（SDD），它使用结构化规范作为权威真相源。本文做出三项贡献。首先，基于经过验证的文献语料库，它识别了无监管对话式生成的失败模式：生产力-可靠性悖论、有限上下文导致的架构侵蚀、安全暴露和技术债务。其次，它引入了规范治理参考模型（SGRM）。这个工具无关的框架定义了四组件规范契约，通过确定性验证约束随机生成，形式化了三个严谨级别，并将生成、验证和治理整合到闭环架构中。第三，它根据ISO/IEC 25010评估了SGRM，将质量特征映射到治理机制。实证证据支持这一点，报告在宪法约束下安全缺陷减少了73%，通过规范治理的代理交付上市时间减少了50%。分析得出结论，虽然氛围编码对于构思和快速原型制作有价值，但企业软件需要规范治理，以将概率性AI生成转化为确定性的、可审计的工程。讨论了边界条件、有效性威胁和未来研究方向。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) and agentic AI are shifting software engineering from manual coding toward intent specification, architecture, and governance. Two paradigms have emerged: vibe coding, an intuition-driven approach accepting AI artifacts via observed behavior, and Specification-Driven Development (SDD), which uses structured specifications as the authoritative source of truth. This article makes three contributions. First, based on a verified literature corpus, it identifies failure modes of ungoverned conversational generation: the productivity-reliability paradox, architectural erosion from limited context, security exposure, and technical debt. Second, it introduces the Specification Governance Reference Model (SGRM). This tool-independent framework defines four-component specification contracts, constrains stochastic generation via deterministic validation, formalizes three rigor levels, and integrates generation, verification, and governance into a closed-loop architecture. Third, it evaluates SGRM against ISO/IEC 25010, mapping quality characteristics to governance mechanisms. Empirical evidence supports this, reporting a 73% reduction in security defects under constitutional constraints and a 50% reduction in time-to-market through specification-governed agentic delivery. The analysis concludes that while vibe coding is valuable for ideation and rapid prototyping, enterprise software requires specification governance to transform probabilistic AI generation into deterministic, auditable engineering. Boundary conditions, threats to validity, and future research directions are discussed.

### [13] [Beyond Visibility and Technical Reuse: Public Application Transformation in Open-Source Model Ecosystems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16687)
*Duorong Wang,Xiaoting Wei,Bin Liu,Jiannan Yang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究通过Hugging Face的大规模数据分析，引入并验证了“公共应用转化”作为衡量开源模型影响的新维度，发现其与平台可见性相关但不等同于技术重用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究仅关注模型发布或技术重用，未能全面衡量模型在公共应用中的实际影响力，因此需要引入公共应用转化这一新维度。

Method: 构建了包含256万模型仓库、106万Spaces等的大规模数据集，利用Model-Space等链接分析公共应用转化，并比较其与下载、点赞等指标的关系。

Result: 公共应用转化高度集中，仅少数模型关联Spaces；应用转化不同于技术重用，且转化后的模型具有更强的元数据就绪性和异构配置。

Conclusion: 公共应用转化是衡量开源模型影响的重要维度，将模型影响从工件可用性和技术重用扩展到平台中介的跨对象转化。

中文摘要：开源模型平台使得发布AI模型更加容易，但仅发布模型并不能揭示模型是否变得可见、被技术重用或融入公共应用。本研究引入公共应用转化作为平台可见的模型影响维度，并通过Hugging Face上的结构化Model-Space链接对其进行检验。我们构建了一个平台规模的数据集，包含256万个模型仓库、106万个Spaces、810,087个数据集仓库和122万个账户资料，以及Model-Space、Dataset-Space和模型间技术重用链接。分析显示，公共应用转化具有高度选择性和集中性：只有一小部分模型与Spaces链接，且大多数Model-Space链接集中在有限的模型上。更重要的是，应用转化与平台可见性相关，但不等同于技术重用，表明下载量、点赞数、下游模型重用和应用层面的采纳捕捉了模型影响的不同形式。额外分析显示，应用转化后的模型倾向于表现出更强的基于元数据的就绪性，并进入包含数据集、SDK和特定任务应用类别的异构Space配置。通过追踪模型从仓库进入公共应用和演示的过程，本研究将开源模型影响的测量从工件可用性和技术重用扩展到跨AI信息对象的平台中介转化。

Original abstract: Open-source model platforms have made it easier to publish AI models, but model release alone does not reveal whether models become visible, technically reused, or incorporated into public applications. This study introduces public application transformation as a platform-visible dimension of model impact and examines it through structured Model-Space links on Hugging Face. We construct a platform-scale dataset of 2.56 million model repositories, 1.06 million Spaces, 810,087 dataset repositories, and 1.22 million account profiles, together with Model-Space, Dataset-Space, and model-to-model technical reuse links. The analysis shows that public application transformation is highly selective and concentrated: only a small share of models are linked to Spaces, and most Model-Space links are concentrated among a limited set of models. More importantly, application transformation is associated with platform visibility but is not equivalent to technical reuse, indicating that downloads, likes, downstream model reuse, and application-facing uptake capture different forms of model impact. Additional analyses show that application-transformed models tend to exhibit stronger metadata-based readiness and enter heterogeneous Space configurations involving datasets, SDKs, and task-specific application categories. By tracing how models move from repositories into public applications and demos, this study extends the measurement of open-source model impact from artifact availability and technical reuse to platform-mediated transformation across AI information objects.

</details>


### [14] [Dependency-Guided Code Generation: Structured Matrix Decomposition and Consistency-Guided Refinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16692)
*Mingqiao Mo,Yangchen Zeng,Zikai Xiao,Xin Xiao,Wenhua Nie,Zhaolu Kang,Guangyuan Dong,Kai Shu,Hao Zhang,Xiaodong Fan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一种依赖感知的代码生成框架，通过分解依赖为量化矩阵和稀疏低秩分解并用交替优化学习，将其作为约束生成代码，在语义和结构上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法无法充分捕捉代码实体间复杂多层次的依赖关系，导致生成代码逻辑不完整或难以集成。

Method: 提出依赖感知框架，用图表示代码实体交互；将依赖分解为量化矩阵（强显式）和稀疏低秩分解（弱隐式），通过交替优化学习；生成时以依赖结构为约束；并引入稀疏三元组表示强依赖以提升效率。

Result: 大量实验表明，所提方法在语义对齐和结构保真度上一致优于现有方法。

Conclusion: 该方法有效提升了代码生成的语义连贯性和结构一致性。

中文摘要：现代软件系统日益增长的复杂性使得自动代码生成成为软件工程中的一项基本任务。然而，现有方法往往无法充分捕捉代码实体间复杂、多层次的依赖关系，导致生成的代码逻辑不完整或难以集成到实际系统中。为解决这一局限，我们提出了一种依赖感知的代码生成框架，通过基于图的表示显式建模代码实体间的交互。我们将依赖分解为两个互补组件：一个量化矩阵用于捕捉强的显式关系，以及一个稀疏低秩分解用于建模较弱的隐式交互。该分解通过交替优化过程高效学习。在代码生成过程中，学习到的依赖结构被作为约束引入，确保生成代码的语义连贯性和结构一致性。此外，我们为强依赖引入了一种稀疏三元组表示，显著提高了存储效率和计算可扩展性。大量实验表明，与现有方法相比，我们的方法一致地生成具有更优语义对齐和结构保真度的代码。

Original abstract: The increasing complexity of modern software systems has made automated code generation a fundamental task in software engineering. However, existing approaches often fail to adequately capture the intricate, multi-level dependencies among code entities, leading to generated code that is logically incomplete or difficult to integrate into real-world systems. To address this limitation, we propose a dependency-aware code generation framework that explicitly models interactions among code entities through a graph-based representation. We decompose dependencies into two complementary components: a quantized matrix that captures strong, explicit relations, and a sparse low-rank factorization that models weaker, implicit interactions. The decomposition is efficiently learned via an alternating optimization procedure. During code generation, the learned dependency structure is incorporated as a constraint, ensuring both semantic coherence and structural consistency of the generated code. Furthermore, we introduce a sparse triplet representation for strong dependencies, significantly improving storage efficiency and computational scalability. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our approach consistently produces code with superior semantic alignment and structural fidelity compared to existing methods.

### [15] [Model-Driven Discipline for Multi-Agent LLMs: Requirement-to-Verification Generation of Traceable System Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16708)
*Ran Wei,Le Zhu,Haochi Wang,Ruizhe Yang,Jiapeng Guan,Siyuan Ji,Yuchen Hu,Zhe Jiang,Xiangyang Ji*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: RADIANT融合MDE与多智能体LLM，自动生成异构模型并实现形式验证，显著减少开发时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 克服典型MDE中因多工具和异构模型导致的可追溯性、维护和变更管理困难。

Method: 结合MDE与多智能体LLM，从需求模型自动生成概念模型、领域特定语言、系统模型和行为模型及追踪链接，进行变化影响分析，并将行为模型转为CSP进行形式验证与修复。

Result: 多智能体分解提高了生成工件的语法有效性和可执行性，语义准确性依赖模型；开发时间减少10-15倍，流程可迁移至新领域。

中文摘要：软件复杂性是系统工程师长期面临的挑战。模型驱动工程（MDE）通过将模型视为一级制品来解决这一问题，但典型的MDE过程涉及许多工具，并产生不同系统方面的异构模型，使得可追溯性、维护和变更管理变得困难。我们提出了RADIANT，一种将MDE与多智能体大语言模型（LLM）相结合的工程方法，用于完整的基于模型的系统开发，重点关注安全关键系统。从精心指定的需求模型出发，RADIANT自动生成跨工程阶段的异构模型——概念模型、领域特定建模语言、一致的系统模型和行为模型——以及可执行的元素级可追溯性链接，在此基础上提供精确的自动化变更影响分析。生成的行为模型被转换为CSP并进行了形式化验证（例如死锁自由和收敛性），并带有反例驱动的修复循环。在三个LLM上评估RADIANT，我们发现与单智能体基线相比，多智能体分解可靠地提高了生成形式工件的语法有效性——以及在模型代码生成允许的情况下提高其可执行性——而语义准确性的提升则依赖于模型。一项六名参与者的研究显示开发时间减少了一个数量级（10-15倍），并且未修改的流程可迁移到第二个领域。

Original abstract: Software complexity is a long-standing challenge for system engineers. Model-Driven Engineering (MDE) addresses it by treating models as first-class artefacts, but a typical MDE process spans many tools and produces heterogeneous models of different system aspects, making traceability, maintenance, and change management difficult.
  We propose RADIANT, an engineering methodology that combines MDE with Multi-Agent Large Language Models (LLMs) for complete model-based system development, with a focus on safety-critical systems. From a carefully specified requirement model, RADIANT automatically generates heterogeneous models across engineering phases -- a concept model, a domain-specific modelling language, a conforming system model, and a behaviour model -- together with executable, element-level traceability links, on top of which it provides exact, automated change-impact analysis. Generated behaviour models are translated into CSP and formally verified (e.g.\ for deadlock freedom and convergence) with a counterexample-driven repair loop. Evaluating RADIANT across three LLMs, we find that the multi-agent decomposition reliably improves the \emph{syntactic validity} of the generated formal artefacts over a single-agent baseline -- and their \emph{executability} where the model's code generation permits -- while gains in semantic accuracy are model-dependent. A six-participant study shows an order-of-magnitude ($10$--$15\times$) reduction in development time, and the unmodified pipeline transfers to a second domain.

Understanding these behaviors is critical for identifying how agentic reviewers succeed, fail, and incur hidden operational costs in practice. Then, we analyze the reviewers' behavior based on their trajectories. Our results show that agentic reviewers achieve higher review precision but incur substantial exploration and validation overhead, while successful reviews are associated with stronger planning and less downstream validation. ### [17] [A Preliminary Study on the Impact of AI in the Creativity and Collaboration in Software Teams](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16744)

Original abstract: Generative artificial intelligence (GenAI) tools are reshaping software engineering work, increasingly acting as cognitive partners rather than purely instrumental aids. Most AI tooling remains optimized for individual use, yet software development is inherently collaborative and creative, raising open questions about how AI affects team-based work. This paper examines how software engineering professionals perceive and integrate AI tools focusing on creativity and collaboration within teams. We conducted semi-structured interviews with 13 software professionals from four companies, each representing a distinct team. Our analysis identifies three central themes - AI Use, Consequences of AI, and Collaboration and Team Dynamics, alongside Emotions as a cross-cutting dimension. Key findings include: AI broadens developers' creative repertoires but may narrow independent ideation; developers increasingly consult AI instead of colleagues, weakening peer learning and mentoring; and teams are developing emerging triadic collaboration patterns in which developers, colleagues, and AI reason together.

### [18] [A Non-Intrusive Traffic Analysis Framework for Authorization Risk Detection and Coordinated Response in Web Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16754)
*Siqi Lin,Yuchao Luo,Zihan Zhu,Yiran Wang,Borui Qiu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一种非侵入式流量分析框架，通过多源证据融合和分级决策实现实时授权风险检测与协调响应，在测试中达到99.90%准确率和亚毫秒延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法难以从网络流量中实时识别授权违规，因为此类违规严重依赖业务语义且缺乏明显的协议层特征。

Method: 关联请求-响应事务提取访问主体、端点、对象标识、认证状态和行为序列；将多源证据映射为可解释风险组件；通过加权融合和高风险优先级约束产生分级决策（允许、告警、阻断、外部策略）。

Result: 在2000样本测试中：准确率99.90%，精确率100%，召回率99.80%，F1 99.90%；移除运行时对象证据后F1降至81.31%，移除高风险优先级约束后降至73.90%；原型测试中平均延迟0.077ms，P99延迟0.137ms。

Conclusion: 该框架能在不修改应用代码的情况下组织异构运行时证据并实现可执行的授权风险决策与协调响应，但未证明在生产环境中的普适性。

中文摘要：在有效Web会话下的授权违规很难从流量中实时识别和处理，因为它们严重依赖于业务语义且几乎没有独特的协议级特征。本文提出了一种用于授权风险检测和协调响应的非侵入式流量分析框架。将请求-响应事务关联起来，提取访问主体、业务端点、对象标识符、认证状态和行为序列。将对象访问证据、身份一致性、行为异常、认证上下文、网络环境和端点操作风险映射到可解释的风险组件。加权融合和高风险优先级约束产生分级决策，驱动允许、告警、阻断和外部策略动作。风险组件使用确定性和可解释的规则实例化，以评估框架层面的多源证据组织、风险融合和协调响应循环。在一个包含2000个平衡标记样本的受控本地测试平台上，该框架将1000个授权风险事件中的998个分类为风险，并且在1000个正常访问中没有产生误报，实现了99.90%的准确率、100.00%的精确率、99.80%的召回率和99.90%的F1分数。移除运行时对象证据后，F1分数降至81.31%；移除高风险优先级约束后，F1分数降至73.90%。在一个包含100个并发请求和总共1000个请求的原型可行性测试中，平均风险决策计算延迟为0.077毫秒，P99延迟为0.137毫秒。结果证明了在不修改应用程序代码的情况下组织异构运行时证据并建立可执行的授权风险决策和协调响应循环的可行性，但并未证明在生产环境中的普遍适用性。

Original abstract: Authorization violations under valid Web sessions are difficult to identify and handle in real time from traffic because they depend strongly on business semantics and exhibit few distinctive protocol-level features. This paper proposes a non-intrusive traffic analysis framework for authorization risk detection and coordinated response. Request-response transactions are correlated to extract the access subject, business endpoint, object identifier, authentication state, and behavioral sequence. Object-access evidence, identity consistency, behavioral anomalies, authentication context, network environment, and endpoint-operation risk are mapped to interpretable risk components. Weighted fusion and high-risk priority constraints produce graded decisions that drive allow, alert, block, and external policy actions. The risk components are instantiated using deterministic and interpretable rules to evaluate multi-source evidence organization, risk fusion, and the coordinated-response loop at the framework level. In a controlled local testbed containing 2,000 balanced labeled samples, the framework classified 998 of 1,000 authorization-risk events as risky and produced no false positives among 1,000 normal accesses, achieving 99.90% accuracy, 100.00% precision, 99.80% recall, and a 99.90% F1 score. Removing runtime object evidence reduced the F1 score to 81.31%, while removing the high-risk priority constraint reduced it to 73.90%. In a prototype feasibility test with 100 concurrent requests and 1,000 total requests, mean risk-decision computation latency was 0.077 ms and P99 latency was 0.137 ms. The results demonstrate the feasibility of organizing heterogeneous runtime evidence and establishing an executable authorization-risk decision and coordinated-response loop without modifying application code, but do not establish general applicability in production environments.

</details>


### [19] [When Post-Anchor Metrics Fail: Stabilization Regimes in AI-Evidence Open-Source Projects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16979)
*Hudson Craig,Benjamin Barlog,Chenggang Wang,Longwei Wang,Zedong Peng*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 后锚点稳定密度指标无法有效衡量架构变更导致的延迟稳定义务，因为该指标混淆了普遍维护与真正债务；通过引入稳定机制和人工验证，发现仅有3%的事件可归因于延迟义务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前仓库挖掘研究难以衡量架构变更是否产生延迟稳定义务，需要更精确的度量方法。

Method: 对338个GitHub仓库进行差异级别研究，设计308事件连续窗口实验，并引入六种稳定机制，通过两名独立编码员对100个候选锚点事件进行人工验证。

Result: 后锚点稳定密度指标无效：锚点事件与非锚点对照组密度相近；人工验证显示仅3%的事件是真正的延迟义务，其余由分类器错误、局部强化、后台维护或锚点前强化解释。

Conclusion: 后锚点密度指标不可靠，需要结合稳定机制和受控设计的归因方法才能可靠识别稳定义务。

中文摘要：仓库挖掘研究越来越多地分析AI证据项目，但如何衡量架构变更是否产生延迟稳定义务仍不清楚。一个自然指标——后锚点稳定密度——计算在引入持久边界后出现的测试、CI门控、文档和修复的数量。我们表明该指标无效。在对338个2026年高知名度GitHub仓库的差异级别研究中，锚点很常见（338个中有321个包含真实变更文件锚点证据），但一个受控的308事件连续窗口实验发现没有后锚点提升：广泛和严格的稳定信号均产生中位数后/前密度比率接近1.0，而非锚点对照组同样密集。我们引入稳定机制，即解释密度指标为何失败的六种重复模式，并使用人工验证对其进行校准。两名独立编码员从盲包中标记100个分层候选锚点事件（债务归因的kappa=0.50）。验证揭示了一个两层陷阱：许多候选锚点并非持久边界（100个中有45个），即使在此校准样本中的有效锚点中，无提升结果依然成立：100个事件中仅有3个幸存为可归因的延迟义务；其余97个由分类器错误、锚点局部强化、后台维护或锚点前强化解释。后锚点密度将普遍维护与真正债务混为一谈；在仓库挖掘能够可靠识别稳定义务之前，需要具有机制意识的受控设计进行归因。

Original abstract: Repository mining studies increasingly analyze AI-evidence projects, yet it remains unclear how to measure whether architectural changes create deferred stabilization obligations. A natural metric, post-anchor stabilization density, counts tests, CI gates, documentation, and fixes appearing after a durable boundary is introduced. We show that this metric fails. In a diff-level study of 338 high-visibility 2026 GitHub repositories, anchors are common (321 of 338 contain real changed-file anchor evidence), but a controlled 308-event contiguous-window experiment finds no post-anchor uplift: broad and strict stabilization signals both yield median post/pre density ratios near 1.0, and non-anchor controls are equally dense. We introduce stabilization regimes, six recurring patterns that explain why the density metric fails, and use human validation to calibrate them. Two independent coders label 100 stratified candidate-anchor events from blinded packets (kappa = 0.50 on debt attribution). The validation exposes a two-layer trap: many candidate anchors are not durable boundaries (45 of 100), and even among valid anchors in this calibration sample the no-uplift result holds: only 3 of 100 events survive as attributable delayed obligations; the remaining 97 are explained by classifier error, anchor-local hardening, background maintenance, or pre-anchor hardening. Post-anchor density conflates pervasive maintenance with genuine debt; controlled designs with regime-aware attribution are necessary before repository mining can reliably identify stabilization obligations.

</details>


### [20] [Schema-Bound LLM Control of Scientific Instrumentation through Model Context Protocol Skills](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17012)
*Roberto dos Reis,Vinayak P. Dravid*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出通过MCP连接本地LLM与科学仪器的方法，验证表明可由本地小模型驱动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学仪器难以连接LLM智能体：供应商API限制、云托管禁止、自然语言接口产生不合理参数。

Method: 结合四个要素：模式绑定工具表面（物理验证）、供应商中立适配器模式、持久生命周期、MCP技能注册。

Result: 开源服务器暴露30工具等，120个硬件无关测试全通过，15个集成测试通过12-15个，初步探测显示本地小模型可行。

Conclusion: 提供有边界、可测试、可重复的闭环智能体仪器研究基础。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）能够规划工具介导的科学工作，但科学仪器仍然难以与这类智能体连接：供应商API可能只能加载在采集主机进程内部，设施可能禁止云托管智能体，而自然语言接口可能产生物理上不合理的参数。我们提出了一种通过模型上下文协议（MCP）将本地LLM连接到科学仪器的方法。它结合了：（1）一个模式绑定的工具表面，在适配器调度前根据物理边界验证请求；（2）一个供应商中立、主机进程的适配器模式，将语言端的推理与仪器端的执行分离；（3）用于长时间运行的实时处理作业的持久生命周期；（4）MCP提示注册的技能，将类型化工具组合成可重用的多步骤协议。我们的开源参考服务器通过实现相同协议表面的物理合理模拟器，暴露了30个类型化工具、5种实时作业类型和6项技能。验证纯粹是软件层面的：所有120个硬件无关的测试均确定性通过，而15个本地LLM集成测试在多次运行中通过12-15个（共15个），原因在于模型的非确定性。一个初步的单次运行探测，跨越五个开源工具调用LLM，表明模式绑定接口可以由本地的小型开源模型驱动，无需云依赖；这不是一个基准测试，也没有置信区间。该方法为闭环智能体仪器研究提供了一个有边界、可测试且可重复的基础。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can plan tool-mediated scientific work, but scientific instruments remain difficult to connect to such agents: vendor APIs may load only inside acquisition host processes, facilities may prohibit cloud-hosted agents, and natural-language interfaces can emit physically unreasonable arguments. We present a method for connecting local LLMs to scientific instruments through the Model Context Protocol (MCP). It combines: (1) a schema-bound tool surface that validates requests against physical bounds before adapter dispatch; (2) a vendor-neutral, host-process adapter pattern separating language-side reasoning from instrument-side execution; (3) a persistent lifecycle for long-running live-processing jobs; and (4) MCP-prompt-registered skills that compose typed tools into reusable multi-step protocols. Our open-source reference server exposes 30 typed tools, 5 live-job types, and 6 skills through a physics-plausible simulator implementing the same protocol surface. Validation is software-only: all 120 hardware-independent tests pass deterministically, while 15 local-LLM integration tests pass 12-15 of 15 across runs because of model nondeterminism. A preliminary single-run probe across five open tool-calling LLMs indicates that the schema-bound interface can be driven locally by small open-weight models without cloud dependency; it is not a benchmark and has no confidence intervals. The method provides a bounded, testable, and reproducible foundation for closed-loop agentic instrumentation research.

### [21] [Can LLM Code Explanations Adapt to Diverse Problem-Solvers' Needs?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17022)
*Andrew Anderson,David Piorkowski,Justin Weisz,Margaret Burnett,Kush Varshney*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文首次研究了LLM代码解释如何根据用户的问题解决风格进行语言适配，通过分析六种LLM生成的1,072个解释，发现13种语言适配并贡献了两种适配方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究未考虑LLM代码解释对用户不同问题解决风格的适应，可能导致解释不匹配用户需求，影响生产力和学习。

Method: 基于包容性设计方法开发提示词，从六个开放权重LLM生成1,072个代码解释，使用自然语言处理技术分析语言适配。

Result: 发现13种语言适配的分类体系，并识别了不同LLM在适配频率上的差异。

Conclusion: 本文首次探索问题解决风格适配，贡献了两种适配方法，为个性化代码解释提供了基础。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）的代码解释可以帮助人们解决与代码相关的问题，然而先前的研究表明人们有不同的解决问题的风格。如果解释不能满足人们的解决问题需求，他们可能会在工作中效率降低，并错失学习和成长的机会。尽管一些研究探讨了LLM如何根据用户的年龄或专业知识调整其输出，但尚无先前研究探讨LLM如何根据人们的解决问题风格调整其代码解释。为弥补这一空白，我们根据一种考虑了5种解决问题风格的成熟包容性设计方法开发了提示词，并从六个开放权重LLM生成了1,072个代码解释。利用自然语言处理技术，我们揭示了一个包含13种语言适配的分类体系，每种适配都有来自文献、提示词或LLM输出的证据支持。它们还显示了哪些LLM比其他LLM更频繁地调整其代码解释。本文是首个调查LLM代码解释中解决问题风格适配的研究，贡献了两种解决问题风格适配方法：每种适配的陈述性语句和10个解决问题风格提示词。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM) code explanations can support people in solving code-related problems, yet prior work has shown that people have diverse problem-solving styles. If explanations fail to meet people's problem-solving needs, they may be less productive in their occupations and miss opportunities to learn and grow. Although some research has examined how LLMs can adapt their outputs to a user's age or expertise, no prior work has examined how LLMs can adapt their code explanations to people's problem-solving styles. To address this gap, we developed prompts from an established inclusive design method that considers 5 types of problem-solving styles, and we generated 1,072 code explanations from six open-weight LLMs. Using natural language processing techniques, we uncovered a taxonomy of 13 linguistic adaptations, with each adaptation supported by evidence from the literature, the prompts, or the LLMs' outputs. They also show which LLMs adapted their code explanations more frequently than others. This paper is the first to investigate problem-solving style adaptations in LLM code explanation, contributing two problem-solving adaptation approaches: declarative statements for each adaptation and 10 problem-solving style prompts.

</details>


### [22] [Where Does Agent Reliability Come From? A Cross-Benchmark Decomposition of Verification Loops, Specialist Models, and Scaffolding in a Production Enterprise Agent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17044)
*Arunabh Dastidar*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 针对多步企业智能体任务中单次推理缺乏检查点的问题，本文提出的Leni系统通过验证循环（执行-观察-比较-纠正）和轻量级专用模型，在三个基准上显著提升了性能，并分解出提升主要来自脚手架、路由和专家模型而非验证步骤本身。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多步企业智能体任务中的单次推理缺乏检查点，导致决策后无法纠正错误，需要引入验证机制。

Method: 采用验证循环架构（执行、观察、比较、纠正），配备轻量级任务专用后训练模型；在三个基准测试上评估未修改的生产配置，并通过消融实验分解性能提升来源。

Result: 在SpreadsheetBench、BullshitBench和GAIA验证集上分别提升+11.0、+7~10、约+15个百分点；验证步骤孤立贡献仅+1.5个百分点但集中在高分区间；验证器捕获率0.20，修复率0.75，无误报。

Conclusion: 验证循环的价值主要来自脚手架、路由和专家模型，而非验证步骤本身；验证步骤的有效性依赖于小型专用模型，使用生成性模型会削弱其作用。

中文摘要：多步企业智能体任务以一种特征性的方式失败：单次推理在决定答案和承诺答案之间没有检查点。我们研究了一个生产系统（Leni），其架构安装了这样的检查点：验证循环（执行、观察、比较、纠正），由轻量级任务专用后训练模型配备。我们评估了未修改的生产配置在三个强调不同失败模式的公共基准上的表现：SpreadsheetBench Verified（静默计算错误）、BullshitBench v2（前提虚构）和GAIA验证集（长工具链上的级联错误）。整个系统在其前沿基础模型上提高了：SpreadsheetBench上+11.0个百分点（91.25% vs 80.25%，n=400，p<0.001），BullshitBench上+7至+10个百分点（98% vs 91%，n=100），GAIA验证集上约+15个百分点（75.2% pass@1，n=165；83.0% best-of-k）。我们的核心贡献是对这一提升的分解：大部分来自脚手架、路由和专家模型，而不是来自验证步骤本身，其孤立贡献很小（+1.5个百分点），但集中在分数分布的顶端，在那里它将原本失败的任务转化为成功。我们对循环进行了端到端的测量，得到了一个经验性的验证器混淆矩阵（捕获率约0.20，修复率0.75，无误报回归），这支撑了一个复合可靠性模型。专家模型交换消融实验表明，循环的价值取决于谁在观察：用生成性前沿模型替换小型训练的验证器会消除大部分补救。一个有效前提控制显示，在100个专家级问题中零过度拒绝。

Original abstract: Multi-step enterprise agent tasks fail in a characteristic way: single-pass inference has no checkpoint between deciding an answer and committing to it. We study one production system (Leni) whose architecture installs such checkpoints: verification loops (execute, observe, compare, correct) staffed by lightweight task-specialized post-trained models. We evaluate the unmodified production configuration on three public benchmarks stressing distinct failure modes: SpreadsheetBench Verified (silent computation error), BullshitBench v2 (premise confabulation), and the GAIA validation split (cascade error over long tool chains). The full system improves over its frontier base model by +11.0 percentage points on SpreadsheetBench (91.25% vs 80.25%, n=400, p<0.001), +7 to +10 percentage points on BullshitBench (98% vs 91%, n=100), and roughly +15 points on GAIA validation (75.2% pass@1, n=165; 83.0% best-of-k). Our central contribution is a decomposition of that uplift: most of it comes from scaffolding, routing, and specialist models rather than from the verification step itself, whose isolated contribution is small (+1.5 points) but concentrated at the top of the score distribution, where it converts otherwise-failing tasks. We instrument the loop end-to-end, yielding an empirical verifier confusion matrix (catch rate about 0.20, fix rate 0.75, no false-alarm regressions) that grounds a compounding-reliability model. Specialist-swap ablations suggest that the loop's value depends on who observes it: replacing the small trained verifier with the generating frontier model eliminates most rescues. A valid-premise control shows zero over-rejections in 100 expert-level questions.

</details>


### [23] [MechMem-RTL: Reusing Verified Mechanism Memories for LLM-Based RTL Repair](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17053)
*Mingyu Cheng,Junjie Gao,Jinhua Cui,Kuncai Zhong*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出MechMem-RTL，通过重用验证器确认的修复记录（而非文本相似性）来修复RTL时序逻辑错误，在48个任务上优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于文本相似性的RAG在修复时序逻辑错误时因自然语言无法反映硬件执行语义而误导模型，需要更精确的修复记录重用方法。

Method: MechMem-RTL框架，存储修复记录包含触发证据、故障机制、修复动作等，新故障时仅当验证器证据与存储触发严格兼容时才注入历史记录，否则仅用当前证据。

Result: 在48个时序RTL任务、6个修复模型上，MechMem-RTL以最多两次修复解决了180/288任务-模型对，优于标准反馈（109）和任务相似性RAG（107）。

Conclusion: MechMem-RTL通过重用验证器确认的修复记录有效提升自动修复性能。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）能够自动修复寄存器传输级（RTL）设计。然而，修复复杂的时序逻辑错误需要重用过去的调试经验。现有的检索增强生成（RAG）依赖于任务文本相似性来提供这种经验。这种基于文本的方法常常误导模型，因为自然语言难以反映周期级的硬件执行语义。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了MechMem-RTL，一个重用验证器确认的修复记录而不是文本相似性的修复框架。每个存储的记录严格链接了触发证据、诊断的故障机制、局部修复动作、保持约束和验证摘要。对于新的故障，MechMem-RTL仅在确定性验证器证据与存储的触发证据严格兼容时注入过去的记录。否则，系统仅使用当前的验证器证据。我们在六个修复模型上的48个公共时序RTL任务上评估了MechMem-RTL。每个任务最多进行两次修复尝试，MechMem-RTL成功解决了288个任务-模型对中的180个，优于标准反馈修复（109对）和任务相似性RAG（107对）。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can automatically repair register-transfer-level (RTL) designs. However, fixing complex sequential logic errors requires reusing past debugging experience. Existing retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) relies on task-text similarity to provide this experience. This text-based approach often misguides the model because natural language poorly reflects cycle-level hardware execution semantics. To address this, we present MechMem-RTL, a repair framework that reuses verifier-confirmed repair records instead of text similarity. Each stored record strictly links trigger evidence, a diagnosed failure mechanism, a local repair action, preservation constraints, and a verification summary. For a new failure, MechMem-RTL injects a past record only when deterministic verifier evidence is strictly compatible with the stored trigger. Otherwise, the system uses only current verifier evidence. We evaluate MechMem-RTL on 48 public sequential RTL tasks across six repair models. With at most two repair attempts per task, MechMem-RTL successfully resolves 180 out of 288 task-model pairs, outperforming standard feedback repair (109 pairs) and task-similarity RAG (107 pairs).

</details>


### [24] [Teach it to stop, not just to click](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17136)
*Barada Sahu,Shivesh Pandey*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 单次运行报告计算机使用强化学习具有误导性；跨种子复制显示方差主要来自数据抽取和运行间非确定性，且修复效果受限；发布cua_reliability库并首次实现SA-OPSD更新。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单次运行报告的智能体计算机使用强化学习结果具有误导性，需要通过跨种子复制和方差分解来评估真实可靠性。

Method: 使用验证器引导修复35B的CUA，在五个oracle评分环境中进行方差成分分解，并采用多模态片段聚合在策略自蒸馏（SA-OPSD）更新。

Result: 修复策略成功率受上游方差主导，数据抽取份额占主导（48%）；运行间分布双峰，单次运行约30%失败模式；固定token修复可靠（0.97±0.06），开放式修正仅部分成功；帧级修复仅当修正为唯一障碍时转移成功。

Conclusion: 必须使用跨种子报告才能避免误导性结论；单次改进约有1/3概率符号错误；发布cua_reliability库以促进常规k种子报告。

中文摘要：在单次运行中报告了智能体计算机使用强化学习，但这些数字具有误导性。通过在五个oracle评分环境中使用验证器引导修复一个35B的计算机使用智能体（CUA），我们展示了修复策略的成功率受上游方差主导：跨三个单元格（交叉的数据抽取×种子网格，自助置信区间）的方差成分分解发现评估方差可忽略（σ_eval ≈ 0），训练种子效应在所有地方都很小（≤10%）；相反，方差在数据抽取和运行间非确定性之间分配，数据抽取的份额在最困难的单元格上升至主导地位（48%）。在那里，运行间分布是双峰的（Hartigan dip p=0.07，k=10），因此单次运行大约有30%的概率进入失败模式，均值±标准差是错误的总结。在此基础上，两个发现成立。首先，可修复性在纠正动作的受限程度上是两层的：单个固定token可靠安装（完成检测0.97±0.06），而开放式修正仅是部分的——空间坐标点击（接地0.53±0.35）和生成性字段填充（0.14±0.04）。其次，帧级修复仅在纠正动作是任务唯一剩余障碍时才转移到任务成功（LinkedIn 8/20 vs. 基础0/15，Fisher p=0.006）。我们通过跨种子复制发现了我们自己的两个过度声明——一个样本效率曲线和一个“接地无法购买”的边界；压力测试使得风险外部化：在类似体制下，该领域发表的单次改进大小约有三分之一的概率符号错误。我们发布了一个库（cua_reliability）用于常规k种子报告。据我们所知，该装置是第一个在真实35B CUA策略上进行的多模态片段聚合在策略自蒸馏（SA-OPSD）更新。

Original abstract: Agentic computer-use RL is reported in single runs, and those numbers mislead. Using verifier-guided repair of a 35B computer-use agent (CUA) across five oracle-graded environments, we show a repaired policy's success rate is dominated by upstream variance: a variance-components decomposition across three cells (crossed data-draw $\times$ seed grid, bootstrap CIs) finds evaluation variance negligible ($σ_{\mathrm{eval}} \approx 0$) and the training-seed effect small everywhere ($\leq 10\%$); instead it splits between the data draw and run-to-run nondeterminism, the data draw's share rising to dominant ($48\%$) on the hardest cell. There the run-to-run distribution is bimodal (Hartigan dip $p=0.07$, $k=10$), so a single run has roughly a 30% chance of the failure mode and mean$\pm$std is the wrong summary. On that footing, two findings hold. First, repairability is two-tier in how constrained the corrective action is: a single fixed token installs reliably (done-detection $0.97\pm0.06$), while open-ended corrections are only partial -- spatial-coordinate clicks (grounding $0.53\pm0.35$) and a generative field-fill ($0.14\pm0.04$). Second, the frame-level repair transfers to task success only when the corrective action is the task's sole remaining blocker (LinkedIn 8/20 vs. base 0/15, Fisher $p=0.006$). We caught two of our own over-claims -- a sample-efficiency curve and a 'grounding cannot be bought' boundary -- only by replicating across seeds; a stress test makes the stakes external: a single-run improvement of the size this field publishes would have the wrong sign roughly one-third of the time in a comparable regime. We release a library (cua_reliability) for routine k-seed reporting. The apparatus is, to our knowledge, the first multimodal segment-aggregated on-policy self-distillation (SA-OPSD) update on a real 35B CUA policy.

### [25] [SynH-Rank: Quality-Aware Code Search via Diverse Data Synthesis and Hierarchical Ranking Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17139)
*Keyu Liang,Haoye Wang,Yanfu Yan,Zhiyuan Wan,Zhongxin Liu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出SynH-Rank框架，通过LLM驱动的数据合成和分层排名训练实现质量感知代码重排序，并引入新基准和指标，显著提升高质量代码的优先排序能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码重排序器只关注语义相关性而忽略执行速度、内存使用等非功能质量，且缺乏质量标注数据，标准对比学习无法区分高质量与低质量代码的排序关系。

Method: SynH-Rank框架，包括LLM驱动的多样化数据合成生成质量注释数据，以及分层排名训练，使用三级标签（高质量相关 > 低质量相关 > 不相关）显式建模质量层次。

Result: 在QPA指标上比骨干模型提升20.15%，比标准相关性对比训练提升15.80%，同时改善传统相关性指标和多条件泛化能力。

Conclusion: SynH-Rank有效实现了质量感知代码搜索，优于现有仅关注相关性的方法。

中文摘要：代码搜索通过实现高效的代码复用来提高开发者的生产力。当前的代码搜索系统通常采用检索-然后-重排序的流水线，其中重排序器专注于建模查询与代码之间的语义相关性。然而，这些重排序器忽略了关键的非功能性质，如执行速度、内存使用和可维护性，而这些对于实际软件开发至关重要。研究表明，开发者期望结果保持高编码标准并满足特定需求（如资源优化），这凸显了质量感知代码搜索的重要性。实现质量感知代码搜索面临两大挑战：缺乏质量标注数据集以进行有效训练，以及标准对比学习目标的局限性，这些目标无法捕捉高质量、低质量和不相关代码之间的排序关系。尽管对比学习擅长区分相关与不相关代码，但其二元目标不支持细微的质量区分。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了SynH-Rank，一个质量感知的代码重排序框架，结合了LLM驱动的多样化数据合成与分层排名训练。SynH-Rank采用三级标签方案显式建模层次结构：高质量相关 > 低质量相关 > 不相关。此外，我们引入了一个包含4,209个对的新基准和两个新指标：质量偏好准确性（QPA）用于评估对高质量代码的优先排序，以及多条件准确性（MCA）用于评估在复杂约束下的性能。实验结果表明，SynH-Rank在QPA上比骨干模型提高了20.15%，比标准的仅相关性对比训练提高了15.80%，同时增强了传统的相关性指标和多条件泛化能力。

Original abstract: Code search enhances developer productivity by enabling efficient code reuse. Current code search systems often use a retrieve-then-rerank pipeline, where rerankers focus on modeling semantic relevance between queries and code. However, these rerankers overlook critical non-functional qualities like execution speed, memory usage, and maintainability, which are essential for practical software development. Studies reveal developers expect results to maintain high coding standards and satisfy specific needs, such as resource optimization, highlighting the importance of quality-aware code search.
  Achieving quality-aware code search faces two major challenges: the scarcity of quality-annotated datasets for effective training and the limitations of standard contrastive learning objectives, which fail to capture the ordinal relationships among high-quality, low-quality, and irrelevant code. Although contrastive learning excels in distinguishing relevant from irrelevant code, its binary objective does not support nuanced quality distinctions.To address these challenges, we propose SynH-Rank, a quality-aware code reranking framework that combines LLM-driven diverse data synthesis with hierarchical ranking training. SynH-Rank employs a three-level labeling scheme to explicitly model the hierarchy: high-quality relevant > low-quality relevant > irrelevant. Additionally, we introduce a new benchmark with 4,209 pairs and two novel metrics: Quality Preference Accuracy (QPA) for assessing prioritization of high-quality code and Multi-Condition Accuracy (MCA) for evaluating performance under complex constraints.Experimental results show SynH-Rank improves QPA by 20.15\% over backbone models and outperforms standard relevance-only contrastive training by 15.80\%, while simultaneously enhancing traditional relevance metrics and multi-condition generalizability.

### [26] [Prefactory: Automated Discovery and Application of Library-Adoption Refactorings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17211)
*Islem Bouzenia,Michael Pradel*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Prefactory利用LLM合成搜索启发式而非重复提示，自动发现并重构Python代码中可替换为库API调用的手写实现，在基准测试中显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具只能处理少量手动指定的模式，LLM成本高且难以规模化应用，而许多库采纳机会难以自动发现。因此需要一种自动化、可扩展的方法。

Method: Prefactory先收集库元数据和项目词汇，生成词法和结构检测器；扫描候选函数后启发式排序；为高分候选函数用LLM生成重构，并通过项目测试和差分测试验证。

Result: 在PrefactoryBench上，Prefactory在文件级检测到75个实例，函数级56个，优于最强基线Codex CLI的35和32；从56个函数中产生40个经测试验证的重构。

Conclusion: Prefactory有效实现了库采纳重构的自动化，检测和验证结果均显著优于现有方法，提供了一种可扩展的解决方案。

中文摘要：用库API调用替换手写代码是一种常见的重构，可以减少代码量、使代码更地道，并复用经过良好测试的实现。然而，许多库采纳的机会难以自动发现：原始代码通常不提及目标库，并且可能仅在行为上与库API相似，句法重叠很少。现有工具，如linter和静态现代化器，只能覆盖一小部分手动指定的模式。而LLM和基于LLM的智能体可以泛化到更多模式，但成本高、难以复现且难以系统化大规模应用。本文介绍了Prefactory，一种用于Python中库采纳重构的自动化方法。关键思想是使用LLM合成可执行的搜索启发式，而不是依赖对代码库的重复LLM提示。给定一个目标项目和一个目标库名，Prefactory收集库元数据和项目词汇，然后生成词法检测器和结构检测器。Prefactory在扫描阶段执行检测器以找到候选函数。然后启发式地对候选函数进行排名，使用LLM为排名最高的函数生成重构，并通过项目测试和新生成的差分测试验证结果。我们在PrefactoryBench上评估Prefactory，这是一个包含来自61个开源Python项目和18个库的100个真实世界库采纳重构的基准测试。Prefactory在文件级别检测到75个实例，在函数级别检测到56个实例，而最强基线（Codex CLI）分别只有35个和32个。从56个检测到的函数中，Prefactory生成了40个经过测试验证的重构。

Original abstract: Replacing hand-written code with library API calls is a common refactoring that can reduce code size, make code more idiomatic, and reuse well-tested implementations. Yet many library-adoption opportunities are hard to find automatically: the original code often does not mention the target library and may resemble the library API only in behavior, with little syntactic overlap. Existing tools, such as linters and static modernizers, cover only a small set of manually specified patterns. LLMs and LLM-based agents, on the other hand, can generalize to more patterns, but they are costly, difficult to reproduce and to apply systematically at scale. This paper introduces Prefactory, an automated approach for library-adoption refactoring in Python. The key idea is to use an LLM to synthesize executable search heuristics rather than relying on repeated LLM prompting over a codebase. Given a target project and a target library name, Prefactory collects library metadata and project vocabulary, then generates lexical and structural detectors. Prefactory executes the detectors during a scan phase to find candidate functions. It then heuristically ranks the candidate functions, generates refactorings for the highest-ranked ones using an LLM, and validates the results with project tests and newly generated differential tests. We evaluate Prefactory on PrefactoryBench, a benchmark of 100 real-world library-adoption refactorings from 61 open-source Python projects and 18 libraries. Prefactory detects 75 instances at the file level and 56 at the function level, compared with 35 and 32 for the strongest baseline (Codex CLI). From the 56 detected functions, Prefactory produces 40 test-validated refactorings.

### [27] [Specifying the Delegated-Autonomy Boundary: Requirements Engineering for Agentic AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17225)
*Chetan Arora,Andreas Vogelsang,Abbi Sharma*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出代理合理性记录和代理委托策略两种构件，以解决代理型AI系统中的委托自主边界问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前代理型AI系统的需求工程未充分处理委托自主边界，相关决策被隐藏在低级实现中。

Method: 提出代理合理性记录（AJR）和代理委托策略（ADP），其中ADP包括目的、权限、信息、协调、保证和演进，且权限为分级模型。

Result: 通过安全关键的医院出院协调代理和自动化代码审查代理两个示例展示了框架的适用性。

中文摘要：代理型AI系统不仅进行预测或推荐；它们还进行规划、维护状态，并以不同程度的自主性在外部环境中行动。这以一种特定且未充分解决的方式改变了需求工程问题：它引入了我们所谓的委托自主边界——即关于哪些决策可以委托给系统、在何种分级权限下、以何种监督方式以及如何返回控制权的决策集合。当前实践将这些决策隐藏在提示词、工具模式及运行时策略中，尽管它们是需求层面的承诺。本文提出了两种互补的构件。首先，代理合理性记录（AJR）帮助团队确定何时使用代理比简单替代方案更合理。其次，代理委托策略（ADP）捕捉了安全有效开发所需指定的内容：目的、权限、信息、协调、保证和演进。关键是，ADP中的权限被建模为分级的，即分层结构。我们通过两个对比示例来阐述该框架：一个安全关键的医院出院协调代理和一个自动化代码审查代理。

Original abstract: Agentic AI systems do not just predict or recommend; they plan, maintain state, and act in external environments with varying degrees of autonomy. This changes the requirements engineering problem in a specific and under-addressed way: it introduces what we call the delegated-autonomy boundary -- the set of decisions about what may be delegated to the system, under what graduated authority, with what oversight, and how control is returned. Current practices bury these decisions inside prompts, tool schemas, and runtime policies, even though they are requirements-level commitments. This paper proposes two complementary artifacts. First, an Agency Justification Record (AJR) helps teams decide when an agent is warranted over simpler alternatives. Second, an Agentic Delegation Policy (ADP) captures what must be specified for safe and effective development: purpose, authority, information, coordination, assurance, and evolution. Crucially, authority in the ADP is modelled as graduated, i.e., a tiered structure. We illustrate the framework with two contrasting examples: a safety-critical hospital discharge coordination agent and an automated code review agent.

</details>

### [29] [A Large-Scale Measurement of AI Bill of Materials Completeness in Hugging Face Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17242)
*Md Erfan,Ahmed Ryan,Md Rayhanur Rahman*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过分析Hugging Face上的约97.5K个AIBOM工件，发现生成的AIBOM在结构上完整，但在AI特定文档（如模型卡、负责任使用、环境等）方面完整性不足。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模型仓库提供的机器可读文档不完整，导致AI供应链存在透明度和治理缺口，AIBOM旨在通过记录AI工件信息来解决这些问题。

Method: 以Hugging Face模型仓库为案例，抽取约97.5K个AIBOM工件，评估其结构字段、模型身份、许可证、外部引用、模型卡文档（数据集、局限性、安全、环境）等完整性，并分析不同仓库和工件特征下的覆盖差异。

Result: 生成的AIBOM在所需结构字段上完全覆盖，但模型卡、元数据、负责任使用、环境、局限性和描述字段覆盖不足或缺失。

Conclusion: 需要改进模型卡实践、增强仓库级可追溯性并开发自动化AIBOM验证工具，以推动更完整AIBOM的生成和采用。

中文摘要：预训练的机器学习（ML）模型帮助开发者无需从头训练模型即可构建ML密集型软件系统。然而，模型仓库通常提供不完整的机器可读文档，涉及模型来源、许可证、数据集、局限性和外部引用，从而在AI供应链中造成透明度和治理缺口。人工智能物料清单（AIBOM）通过记录AI工件（包括模型、元数据、许可证、数据集、模型卡信息和外部引用）来解决这些缺口。以公开的Hugging Face（HF）模型仓库为案例，本文实证研究了AIBOM的完整性，即仓库为机器可读的AI供应链文档提供AIBOM相关信息的程度。我们检查了约97.5K个AIBOM工件，以评估生成的AIBOM在以下方面的完整性：（i）包含所需的结构和元数据字段，（ii）表示模型身份、许可证和外部引用信息，（iii）捕获模型卡文档，如数据集、局限性、安全风险评估和环境信息，（iv）在仓库和工件特征（如任务、许可证可用性、数据集声明、模型家族和论文引用）之间文档覆盖范围的差异。结果表明，生成的AIBOM在所需结构上提供了完整覆盖，但在AI特定文档完整性方面有限。所需字段完全呈现，但模型卡、元数据、负责任使用、环境、局限性和有意义的描述字段在生成的工件中仍然表现不足或缺失。我们的发现激励改进模型卡实践、仓库级可追溯性和自动化AIBOM验证，以推进更完整AIBOM的生成和采用。

Original abstract: Pretrained machine learning (ML) models help developers build ML-intensive software systems without training models from scratch. However, model repositories often provide incomplete machine-readable documentation about model provenance, licenses, datasets, limitations, and external references, creating transparency and governance gaps across the AI supply chain. Artificial Intelligence Bills of Materials (AIBOMs) address these gaps by documenting AI artifacts, including models, metadata, licenses, datasets, model-card information, and external references. Taking public Hugging Face (HF) model repositories as a case study, this paper empirically investigates AIBOM completeness, defined as the extent to which repositories provide AIBOM-relevant information for machine-readable AI supply-chain documentation. We examine approximately 97.5K AIBOM artifacts to assess the extent to which generated AIBOMs: (i) contain required structural and metadata fields, (ii) represent model identity, license, and external-reference information, (iii) capture model-card documentation such as datasets, limitations, safety-risk assessment, and environmental information, and (iv) vary in documentation coverage across repository and artifact characteristics such as task, license availability, dataset declaration, model family, and paper reference. Results indicate that generated AIBOMs provide complete coverage of required AIBOM structure but limited AI-specific documentation completeness. Required fields are fully represented, but model-card, metadata, responsible-use, environmental, limitation, and meaningful-description fields remain weakly represented or missing across generated artifacts. Our findings motivate improved model-card practices, repository-level traceability, and automated AIBOM validation to advance the generation and adoption of more complete AIBOMs.

### [30] [IssueExec: A Test-Driven Approach for Localizing Software Engineering Issues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17286)
*Jiawei Liu,Yun Lin,Chenyan Liu,Yu Qian,Yiming Liu,Jiaxin Chang,Weinan Zhang,Linpeng Huang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出IssueExec方法，利用测试套件作为需求代理，通过领域知识增强表示和分层轨迹分析解决语义鸿沟和噪声问题，在SWE-bench Lite上显著提升问题定位性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有问题定位方法因描述与代码间的抽象鸿沟而效果不佳；理论分析和实证表明测试套件可减少定位不确定性，但存在语义鸿沟和执行噪声两个关键挑战。

Method: IssueExec方法：1) 通过领域知识增强测试表示桥接问题描述与测试标识符的语义鸿沟；2) 采用分层轨迹分析过滤基础设施代码引入的执行噪声。

Result: 在SWE-bench Lite上，函数级Recall@1比最强基线提升41.57%；集成到Agentless流程后，多解决17.72%的问题。

Conclusion: IssueExec通过有效利用测试套件信号实现了问题定位的领先性能，并带来实际的下游改进。

中文摘要：问题定位是从问题描述中识别需要修改的代码位置，是自动化软件维护的关键步骤。现有方法主要试图将问题描述与代码元素直接对齐，但由于问题描述与代码实现之间固有的抽象鸿沟，常常难以奏效。寻求替代信号，我们的理论分析表明，测试套件可以作为需求的可执行代理，平均将定位不确定性降低7.73比特的熵。一项对18个仓库的大规模实证研究验证了这一前提：现有测试覆盖了96.98%的真实文件，并且在82.4%的情况下，两跳路径比直接匹配产生更强的语义连通性。尽管具有潜力，利用测试进行定位面临两个关键挑战：问题描述与测试标识符之间的语义鸿沟，以及来自基础设施代码的执行轨迹中的大量噪声。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了IssueExec，它通过领域知识增强的测试表示来弥合语义鸿沟，并通过分层轨迹分析来过滤噪声。在SWE-bench Lite上的实验表明，IssueExec实现了最先进的性能，在函数级别的Recall@1上比最强基线提高了41.57%。当集成到Agentless流程中时，IssueExec解决了17.72%更多的问题，展示了实际的下游收益。

Original abstract: Issue localization, which identifies code locations requiring modification from issue descriptions, is a critical step in automated software maintenance. Existing approaches predominantly attempt to directly align issue descriptions with code elements, yet often struggle due to the inherent abstraction gap between the issue description and code implementation. Seeking alternative signals, our theoretical analysis suggests that test suites can serve as executable proxies for requirements, reducing localization uncertainty by 7.73 bits of entropy on average. A large-scale empirical study on 18 repositories validates this premise: existing tests cover 96.98\% of ground-truth files, and the two-hop pathway yields stronger semantic connectivity than direct matching in 82.4\% of cases. Despite their potential, leveraging tests for localization faces two key challenges: the semantic gap separating issue descriptions from test identifiers, and the substantial noise in execution traces from infrastructure code. To address these, we propose IssueExec, which bridges the semantic gap through domain-knowledge-enhanced test representations and filters noise via hierarchical trace analysis. Experiments on SWE-bench Lite show that IssueExec achieves state-of-the-art performance, improving function-level Recall@1 by 41.57\% over the strongest baseline. When integrated into the Agentless pipeline, IssueExec resolves 17.72\% more issues, demonstrating practical downstream benefits.

### [31] [Portable models as a replacement for industrial heuristics in compiler optimizations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17389)
*Fot Nikolai,Vinarsky Alexander*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一个可移植的内联预测框架，利用生产编译器诊断作为监督，通过特征提取和模型训练，在轻量级系统中预测函数内联决策。在十五个开源C项目的评估中，CatBoost模型达到ROC-AUC 0.928和PR-AUC 0.713。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在紧凑编译器、源到源工具和解释器中，无法重用GCC或LLVM的优化基础设施，需要将成熟的内联启发式方法转移到轻量级系统。

Method: 提出可移植的内联预测框架：使用生产编译器诊断作为监督，通过提取器重建调用点，准备无菌代码片段，规范化为通用AST，可选降级为轻量级结构IR，导出标量特征用于训练，并将预测器作为C代码输出。

Result: 在十五个C项目的336,938个调用点数据集上，CatBoost在留一项目验证下达到ROC-AUC 0.928和PR-AUC 0.713；阈值调整后F1从0.670提升至0.729，假阳性率从0.192降至0.084。

Conclusion: 提出的可移植内联预测框架能够有效预测内联决策，主要信号来自源代码局部性、显式内联意图、被调用者大小等特征，适用于轻量级系统。

中文摘要：本文研究了在无法重用GCC或LLVM优化基础设施的紧凑编译器、源到源工具和解释器中预测函数内联决策的可能性。这项工作的相关性取决于需要将成熟的内联启发式方法转移到具有有限编译器基础设施、受限运行时依赖性和减少对目标特定分析访问的系统。现有的生产编译器已经包含强大的内联器，但它们的决策依赖于内部中间表示（IR）、遍序、目标模型和分析栈，这些在轻量级系统中难以复现。为了克服这些限制，我们提出了一个可移植的内联预测框架。生产编译器诊断作为监督；一个单独提取器重建调用者-被调用者调用点，准备无菌源代码片段，将它们规范化为通用AST，可选地降级为轻量级结构IR，并导出标量特征用于模型训练。因此，训练好的预测器可以作为普通C代码发出，无需编译器运行时依赖。为了评估所提出的框架，我们构建了一个数据集，包含来自十五个开源C项目的336,938个调用点，包括79,287个编译器报告的内联事件。使用项目感知验证对几个表格模型进行了比较。在留一项目验证下，CatBoost达到了ROC-AUC 0.928和PR-AUC 0.713；阈值调整后，F1从0.670提高到0.729，假阳性率从0.192下降到0.084。特征分析表明，大多数信号集中在源代码位置、显式内联意图、被调用者大小、副作用、分支和调用结构、签名形状以及调用点参数形状上。

Original abstract: The paper investigates the possibility of predicting function-inlining decisions in compact compilers, source-to-source tools, and interpreters where the reuse of GCC or LLVM optimization infrastructure is impractical. The relevance of this work is determined by the need to transfer mature inlining heuristics to systems with limited compiler infrastructure, restricted runtime dependencies, and reduced access to target-specific analysis. Existing production compilers already contain strong inliners, but their decisions depend on internal intermediate representations (IRs), pass ordering, target models, and analysis stacks that are difficult to reproduce in lightweight systems. To overcome these constraints, we propose a portable inlining-prediction framework. Production compiler diagnostics serve as supervision; a separate extractor reconstructs caller-callee callsites, prepares sterile source snippets, normalizes them into a universal AST, optionally lowers them to a lightweight structural IR, and exports scalar features for model training. Thus, a trained predictor can be emitted as ordinary C code without a compiler-runtime dependency. To evaluate the proposed framework, we constructed a dataset comprising 336,938 callsites from fifteen open-source C projects, including 79,287 compiler-reported inline events. A comparison of several tabular models is performed using project-aware validation. Under leave-one-project-out validation, CatBoost reaches ROC-AUC 0.928 and PR-AUC 0.713; after threshold tuning, F1 improves from 0.670 to 0.729 and the false-positive rate drops from 0.192 to 0.084. Feature analysis shows that most signal is concentrated in source locality, explicit inline intent, callee size, side effects, branch and call structure, signature shape, and callsite argument shape.
