### [63] [RECON: Benchmarking Agent Memory for Compositional Reasoning over Long Contexts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16716)
*Mihir Shriniwas Arya*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 专为agent记忆设计的推理基准，评估长上下文组合推理，直接相关agent评测。

TL;DR: RECON是一个评估长上下文组合推理的基准测试，涵盖三个领域24个案卷，测试六类记忆任务，发现最强非Oracle系统准确率仅22.4%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准只评估事实检索或变化检测，缺乏对变化后推理链的追踪能力。

Method: 构建24个案卷，涉及刑事、医疗和金融领域，每个案卷50k-100k tokens，设计六类记忆密集型任务。

Result: 最强非Oracle系统准确率22.4%，检索和推理均构成主要挑战。

Conclusion: 当前架构在记忆密集型推理上存在显著局限，需要改进。

中文摘要：大型语言模型和基于LLM的智能体被广泛用作个人聊天助手、企业副驾驶和自主工作流智能体。在所有这类应用中，记忆（在长上下文和多次交互中积累的信息的保留、访问和推理能力）在决定任何智能体的可靠性中起着关键作用。我们引入了RECON（通过混淆叙事进行扩展上下文推理），一个用于评估长上下文中组合推理的基准测试。RECON涵盖三个领域（刑事、医疗和金融）的24个案卷，每个案卷包含5万到10万个token，并在六项记忆密集型任务上测试智能体：重构多跳证据链、传播级联无效化、解决源冲突、反事实推理、满足时间约束和时间事实检索。最近的记忆基准测试评估智能体是否能检索分散的事实或检测事实是否发生变化，而RECON则评估变化发生后会发生什么，智能体是否能追踪哪些下游结论受到影响，哪些通过独立支持存活，以及替代时间线将如何展开。我们的评估揭示了当前架构的显著局限性：即使是最强的非Oracle系统也仅达到22.4%的准确率，检索和推理各自都是挑战。

Original abstract: Large language models and LLM-based agents are widely used as personal chat assistants, enterprise copilots, and autonomous workflow agents. In all these applications, memory (the ability to retain, access, and reason over information accumulated over long contexts and multiple interactions) plays a crucial role in determining the reliability of any agent. We introduce RECON (Reasoning over Extended Contexts with Obfuscated Narratives), a benchmark for evaluating compositional reasoning over long contexts. RECON spans 24 case files across three domains (criminal, medical, and financial), each ranging from 50k to 100k tokens, and tests agents on six memory intensive tasks: reconstructing multi-hop evidence chains, propagating cascading invalidations, resolving source conflicts, counterfactual reasoning, satisfying temporal constraints, and temporal fact retrieval. Recent memory benchmarks evaluate whether agents can retrieve scattered facts or detect if a fact has changed whereas RECON evaluates what happens after the change, whether agents can trace which downstream conclusions are affected, which survive through independent support, and how alternative timelines would have unfolded. Our evaluation reveals substantial limitations across current architectures: even the strongest non-Oracle system reaches only 22.4% Accuracy, with retrieval and reasoning each surfacing as challenges.

### [64] [Constraint-Anchored Reasoning Traces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16727)
*Zehua Cheng,Wei Dai,Jiahao Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出约束锚定推理轨迹，通过符号约束减少错误传播，可提升agent推理稳定性。

TL;DR: 提出约束锚定推理轨迹（CART）框架，通过交织符号约束断言和回溯机制，将MLLM的错误雪崩率从0.65降至0.14，并提升多项基准性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自回归MLLM存在错误雪崩问题，早期错误导致后续推理全面失败，现有缓解方法缺乏符号基础、错误检测滞后或牺牲自然语言灵活性。

Method: CART将自然语言推理与符号约束断言交织，利用约束传播模块（神经基础头+布尔传播）实时验证一致性，检测矛盾时回溯至最近一致状态，并通过可变频率发射控制锚点密度。

Result: 在五个基准上，雪崩率从0.65降至0.14，GQA准确率提升+4.6%，POPE-all F1达89.1，推理开销≤18%。

Conclusion: CART通过神经符号结合有效抑制错误传播，在保持低开销的同时显著提升多模态推理的鲁棒性和准确性。

中文摘要：自回归多模态大语言模型（MLLM）存在错误雪崩问题：早期推理链（CoT）中的单个错误推理会破坏所有下游推理。我们发现，在最先进的开源MLLM中，一旦首次错误发生，推理会在65%的情况下级联失败（我们称之为雪崩率）。现有的缓解措施——采样多条链、事后自我验证或完整程序合成——要么缺乏符号基础，要么捕捉错误太晚，要么牺牲了自然语言推理的灵活性。我们提出了约束锚定推理轨迹（CART），这是一个神经符号框架，训练MLLM将自然语言推理步骤与符号约束断言（例如，count(red_objects) = 3）交织在一起。一个双管齐下的约束传播模块——结合了学习到的神经基础头与布尔约束传播——持续验证这些锚点与提取的视觉特征，并检查它们之间的逻辑一致性。当检测到矛盾时，回溯控制器停止生成并回退到最后一个一致检查点，防止错误传播。一个可变频率发射机制允许模型自适应控制锚点密度，避免轨迹膨胀。我们通过使用场景图派生的真实约束注释增强GQA、CLEVR-CoGenT和VCR，构建了218K训练实例，并通过LoRA微调了开源MLLM（LLaVA-NeXT、Qwen2-VL）。在五个基准上，CART将雪崩率从0.65降低到0.14，在GQA准确率上比仅训练基线提高了+4.6个百分点，并在POPE-all上实现了89.1的F1分数，推理开销最多为18%。

Original abstract: Autoregressive multimodal large language models (MLLMs) suffer from error snowballing: a single incorrect inference early in a chainof-thought (CoT) trace corrupts all downstream reasoning. We find that in state-of-the-art open-source MLLMs, once the first error occurs, the reasoning cascades into failure across all remaining steps in 65% of such cases (a metric we term the snowball rate). Existing mitigations-sampling multiple chains, post-hoc self-verification, or full program synthesis-either lack symbolic grounding, catch errors too late, or sacrifice the flexibility of natural language reasoning. We propose Constraint-Anchored Reasoning Traces (CART), a neuro-symbolic framework that trains MLLMs to interleave natural language reasoning steps with symbolic constraint assertions: lightweight, machine-checkable statements about visual content (e.g., count(red_objects) = 3). A dual-pronged Constraint Propagation Module-combining a learned neural grounding head with Boolean Constraint Propagation-continuously verifies these anchors against extracted visual features and checks their mutual logical consistency. When a contradiction is detected, a backtrack controller halts generation and reverts to the last consistent checkpoint, preventing error propagation. A variable-frequency emission mechanism allows the model to adaptively control anchor density, avoiding trace bloat. We construct 218K training instances by augmenting GQA, CLEVR-CoGenT, and VCR with ground-truth constraint annotations derived from scene graphs, and fine-tune open-source MLLMs (LLaVA-NeXT, Qwen2-VL) via LoRA. On five benchmarks, CART reduces the snowball rate from 0.65 to 0.14, improves GQA accuracy by +4.6 percentage points over trainingonly baselines, and achieves 89.1 F1 on POPE-all with at most 18% inference overhead.

</details>

*Paul Wittlinger,Giacomo Acitelli,Anti Alman,Fabrizio Maria Maggi,Andrea Marrella*

中文摘要：AI增强的业务流程管理系统（ABPMS）通过利用先进的AI技术来定义、执行和监控复杂流程结构，从而增强了传统的BPMS。在此背景下，框架自主性指的是系统在严格遵守预定框架（即可能跨越多个视角的一组约束）的同时，自主推进业务流程实例执行的能力。现有关于框架自主性的研究主要集中在控制流约束上，无论是声明式还是程序式，并且通常依赖于将这些约束转换为基于自动机的表示。在本研究中，我们通过引入一种新的假设分析工具来扩展这一工作，该工具用多视角约束（包括数据感知和时间条件）增强了流程框架。给定部分流程执行，所提出的方法利用这个增强的框架来推荐符合底层流程规范的最优延续。此外，我们还报告了一项实证评估，证明了该技术的可扩展性和有效性，从而突显了其在ABPMS中支持自主且受约束决策的潜力。

Original abstract: AI-Augmented Business Process Management Systems (ABPMS) enhance traditional BPMS by leveraging advanced AI techniques to define, execute, and monitor complex process structures. Within this landscape, Framed Autonomy denotes the capability of a system to autonomously advance the execution of a Business Process (BP) instance while strictly adhering to a predefined frame, i.e., a set of constraints that may span multiple perspectives. Existing research on framed autonomy has predominantly focused on control-flow constraints, either declarative or procedural, and typically relies on their transformation into automata-based representations. In this study, we extend this line of work by introducing a novel tool for what-if analysis that augments the process frame with multi-perspective constraints, including data-aware and temporal conditions. Given a partial process execution, the proposed approach exploits this enriched frame to recommend optimal continuations in compliance with the underlying process specifications. We additionally report an empirical evaluation demonstrating the scalability and effectiveness of the technique, thereby highlighting its potential for supporting autonomous and constraint-aware decision making in ABPMS.

### [66] [RELIC: Revealed Principles for Learning Interpretable Composable Skills in Multi-Agent Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16745)
*Nguyen Viet Tuan Kiet,Bui Dinh Pham,Duong Quoc Chinh,Dao Van Tung,Tran Cong Dao,Huynh Thi Thanh Binh*

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖集中优化或共享策略，不适合隐私受限的异构智能体协作。

Result: 实现了跨异构技能智能体的协调而无需共享实现，支持隐私保护。

Conclusion: RELIC为多智能体规划中的隐私保护技能学习和协调提供了新范式。

中文摘要：多智能体规划在智能体必须改进专门的决策技能同时保持其内部实现私有时变得困难得多。这种情形发生在智能体独立开发、公开不同接口和能力、并且必须协调而不共享可执行策略时。先前的研究大多假设集中优化、共享策略访问或共同技能表示，使其不适合隐私受限的合作。我们提出了RELIC，一个通过揭示原则学习可解释和可组合技能的框架。每个智能体通过私有LLM引导搜索来改进自己的程序化技能，而可信协调者仅通过团队级性能来评估提议的更新。成功的行为不广播为代码；相反，它们被抽象为可移植的原则，其他智能体可以在自己的接口中实例化这些原则并与本地策略重组。这实现了协调与实现共享的分离，使得在异构技能签名下的跨智能体迁移成为可能。因此，RELIC为多智能体规划中的隐私保护技能学习和协调引入了一种新范式。

Original abstract: Multi-agent planning becomes substantially harder when agents must improve specialized decision-making skills while keeping their internal implementations private. This regime arises when agents are developed independently, expose different interfaces and capabilities, and must nevertheless coordinate without sharing executable policies. Prior research has largely assumed centralized optimization, shared policy access, or common skill representations, making it poorly suited to privacy-constrained cooperation. We introduce RELIC, a framework for learning interpretable and composable skills via revealed principles. Each agent refines its own programmatic skill through private LLM-guided search, while a trusted orchestrator evaluates proposed updates solely through team-level performance. Successful behaviors are not broadcast as code; instead, they are abstracted into portable principles that other agents can instantiate within their own interfaces and recombine with local strategies. This separates coordination from implementation sharing, enabling cross-agent transfer under heterogeneous skill signatures. RELIC thus introduces a new paradigm for privacy-preserving skill learning and coordination in multi-agent planning.

Original abstract: Scientists at European XFEL conduct experiments that generate very large and complex datasets. The subsequent data analysis is challenging as scientists must combine their domain expertise with facility- and software-specific knowledge scattered across documentation, tools, and support channels. To address this problem, we designed and evaluated an agentic AI system tailored to the scientists' needs and integrated with the high-performance computing environment of European XFEL. Using a design science research approach, we conducted a rapid literature review, a systematic evaluation of 16 AI tools, multiple interviews, a focus group, and a user study with experts at European XFEL to develop and evaluate two prototypes. Our study identifies key knowledge challenges in scientific data analysis, derives requirements for an AI agent that supports knowledge retrieval and source code generation, and proposes design recommendations for a specialized system adaptable to the evolving AI tool landscape. These findings provide guidance for developing maintainable AI support in highly specialized scientific environments.

### [68] [AgentBrew: Lifelong Knowledge Brewing from Strong Teachers to Weak LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16851)
*Yangqin Jiang,Chao Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出将教师经验蒸馏为学生外部记忆的agent方法，属于通用agent自我改进与记忆机制。

TL;DR: AgentBrew通过教师经验蒸馏和外部内存实现无需权重更新或教师访问的LLM代理部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测试时学生能力弱且训练时教师强但不可访问，环境反馈稀疏且笔记需适配弱学生。

Method: 提出AgentBrew，包括Ralph Loop（将学生失败转化为环境验证笔记）和学生感知综合（校准教师知识至弱执行器粒度）。

Result: 在编码、数学和工具使用任务上，AgentBrew产生高效且可部署的LLM代理。

Conclusion: 不对称、无训练的知识酿造范型有效生成能力强的可部署代理。

中文摘要：部署LLM代理通常需要一个紧凑的测试时学生，即使在训练期间有更强的教师可用。我们研究知识酿造：将教师的交互经验提炼到学生持久的外部记忆中。关键的是，这不需要权重更新、专家示范、真实标签或测试时教师访问。这一设置面临两个挑战：环境仅提供稀疏的二值反馈，且教师编写的笔记必须固有地定制为能被明显较弱的学生具体执行。为了解决这些困难，我们提出AgentBrew，包含两个耦合组件。首先，故障触发教师——Ralph Loop通过将学生失败转化为环境验证的笔记来缓解稀疏反馈。其次，学生感知综合将教师知识校准到弱执行器的操作粒度，产生模型特定、可操作的指导。在编码、数学和工具使用任务上的广泛评估和全面消融表明，这种不对称、无需训练的酿造范式产生了高度有能力且可部署的LLM代理。

Original abstract: Deploying LLM agents typically requires a compact test-time student, even if a stronger teacher is available during training. We study knowledge brewing: distilling a teacher's interactive experience into a persistent external memory for the student. Crucially, this requires no weight updates, expert demonstrations, ground-truth labels, or test-time teacher access. This setting poses two challenges: environments provide only sparse, binary feedback, and teacher-authored notes must be inherently tailored to be concretely executable by a substantially weaker student. To address these hurdles, we propose AgentBrew, comprising two coupled components. First, a failure-triggered teacher--Ralph Loop mitigates sparse feedback by transforming student failures into environment-validated notes. Second, student-aware synthesis calibrates teacher knowledge to the weak executor's operational granularity, yielding model-specific, actionable guidance. Extensive evaluations and comprehensive ablations across coding, math, and tool-use tasks demonstrate that this asymmetric, training-free brewing paradigm produces highly capable yet deployable LLM agents.

### [69] [Environment-free Synthetic Data Generation for API-Calling Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16900)
*Seanie Lee,Sanjoy Chowdhury,Chao Jiang,Cheng-Yu Hsieh,Ting-Yao Hu,Alexander T Toshev,Oncel Tuzel,Raviteja Vemulapalli*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出无需环境的合成数据生成方法，用于训练API调用agent，可迁移至coding agent数据生成。

TL;DR: 提出一种无需真实环境的合成数据生成方法，利用LLM作为世界模型模拟API交互，生成高质量轨迹用于训练API调用代理，在AppWorld和OfficeBench上性能显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 收集大规模高质量的API调用轨迹数据需要完整的可执行环境和预填充后端数据库，成为训练代理的可扩展性瓶颈。

Method: 仅用API规范，由LLM生成任务，教师代理解决任务，LLM模拟器生成连贯合成API响应，LLM评审员过滤轨迹。

Result: 在AppWorld和OfficeBench基准上，微调后的模型性能显著提升，证明无需可执行环境即可生成有效监督。

Conclusion: 基于LLM的API模拟是一种实用且可扩展的解决方案，能训练跨多种API生态系统的代理。

中文摘要：训练能调用API的大型语言模型（LLM）代理需要大量高质量的轨迹数据。然而，大规模收集此类数据通常需要完全实现的环境，包括可执行的API和预先填充的真实后端数据库，这成为可扩展性的主要瓶颈。为克服这一问题，我们提出了一种无需环境的数据合成方法，利用LLM作为即时的数字世界模型。仅给定API规范，我们的方法生成模拟代理与有状态环境之间交互的轨迹。具体而言，LLM首先生成可通过所提供API解决的多样化任务。然后，教师代理迭代解决每个任务，同时LLM模拟器根据任务上下文和模拟历史生成连贯的合成API响应。最后，LLM评审员过滤轨迹以确保生成数据集的质量。我们分别在具有挑战性的AppWorld和OfficeBench基准上评估了该方法，这两个基准包含信息检索和状态更改任务。在我们的合成数据上微调模型带来了显著的性能提升，表明无需任何可执行环境即可为API调用代理生成有效的监督信号。我们的结果确立了基于LLM的API模拟作为一种实用的、可扩展的解决方案，用于在不同的API生态系统中训练代理。

Original abstract: Training API-calling large language model (LLM) agents demands massive amounts of high-quality trajectories. However, collecting such data at scale typically requires fully implemented environments with executable APIs and realistic, pre-populated backend databases, creating a major bottleneck for scalability. To overcome this, we propose an environment-free synthetic data generation approach that leverages LLMs as on-the-fly digital world models. Given only API specifications, our method generates trajectories mimicking interactions between an agent and a stateful environment. Specifically, an LLM first generates diverse tasks solvable with the provided APIs. A teacher agent then iteratively solves each task while an LLM simulator generates coherent synthetic API responses conditioned on the task context and simulation history. Finally, an LLM judge filters the trajectories to ensure the quality of the resulting dataset. We evaluate our approach on the challenging AppWorld and OfficeBench benchmarks, which include both information-retrieval and state-changing tasks. Fine-tuning models on our synthetic data yields significant performance gains, demonstrating that effective supervision for API-calling agents can be generated without any executable environment. Our results establish LLM-based API simulation as a practical, scalable solution for training agents across diverse API ecosystems.

</details>

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

Result: 小规模（500-1000）时质量过滤效果不显著，大规模（2000）时TopQ优于随机；错误重试率是关键子维度。

Conclusion: 轨迹级质量评分是可行但依赖规模的杠杆，并提出了代理验证的评估协议。

中文摘要：监督微调（SFT）开放权重的大型语言模型在专家代理轨迹上的应用已成为构建能代码代理而不依赖专有模型的主要方法。一个核心但尚未充分探索的问题是轨迹质量和数量如何共同塑造模型性能。我们对SWE-trajectory数据集（67,074条轨迹，其中32,161条已解决）上对Qwen2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct进行LoRA微调时的轨迹数据过滤进行了系统的实证研究。我们提出了一个二维质量评分框架——效率和风格——并通过16项涵盖策略、规模及消融分析的受控实验进行评估。由于7B规模模型在SWE-bench解决率上接近零，我们采用在保留轨迹上的交叉熵（CE）损失作为主要指标，并通过首次动作生成进行验证：CE损失和ROUGE-L完美秩相关（Spearman ρ = -1.00），有限样本证据支持但并未确凿确立该代理。我们的结果揭示了依赖规模的质量-数量权衡：在小规模下，数据集翻倍（从500到1000）导致CE损失降低约12.7%，而TopQ-Random差距小于1%（Mann-Whitney p > 0.10）；在2000条轨迹时，同一差距扩大至3.6%（p = 0.016）。消融进一步将错误重试率识别为主导子维度，其表现与完整复合指标相当（Δ < 0.2%）。这些发现共同确立了轨迹级质量评分作为可行但依赖规模的杠杆用于代码代理SFT，并为端到端解决率在统计上不可行的场景提供了一种经代理验证的评估协议。

Original abstract: Supervised fine-tuning (SFT) of open-weight LLMs on expert agent trajectories has emerged as a prominent approach to building capable code agents without reliance on proprietary models. A central yet underexplored question is how trajectory quality and quantity jointly shape model performance. We present a systematic empirical study of trajectory data filtering for LoRA fine-tuning of Qwen2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct on the SWE-trajectory dataset (67,074 trajectories, of which 32,161 are resolved). We propose a two-axis quality scoring framework -- Efficiency and Style -- and evaluate it through 16 controlled experiments spanning strategy, scale, and ablation analyses. Since 7B-scale models attain near-zero SWE-bench resolve rates, we adopt cross-entropy (CE) loss on held-out trajectories as the primary metric, validated via first-action generation: CE loss and ROUGE-L are perfectly rank-correlated (Spearman $ρ$ = -1.00), with limited-sample evidence supporting but not conclusively establishing this proxy. Our results reveal a scale-dependent quality-quantity trade-off: at small scales, doubling the dataset (500 to 1,000) yields ~12.7% CE-loss reduction whereas the TopQ-Random gap stays <1% (Mann-Whitney p > 0.10); at 2,000 trajectories this same gap widens to 3.6% (p = 0.016). Ablation further identifies error-retry rate as the dominant sub-dimension, performing comparably to the full composite ($Δ$ < 0.2%). Together, these findings establish trajectory-level quality scoring as a viable but scale-sensitive lever for code-agent SFT and offer a proxy-validated evaluation protocol for the regime where end-to-end resolve rate is statistically infeasible.

</details>


### [71] [Lomekwi: Resource-Bounded Tool Discovery in LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16961)
*Roshan Klein-Seetharaman,Daniel Wang,Andrew Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究agent工具发现能力，分解为好奇、识别、效率三个维度，对工具使用agent有启发。

TL;DR: 本文将工具发现分解为好奇心、识别和效率，并发现识别能力与模型大小呈反比缩放。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具使用基准只报告单一成功率，未能区分工具使用和工具发现的不同方面。

Method: 借鉴认知科学，将工具发现分解为好奇心、识别和效率三个维度，并在Voyager等任务中应用，同时设计组合游戏和真实世界模拟环境进行分析。

Result: 识别能力与模型大小呈反比缩放，并在组合游戏和模拟真实世界任务的环境中得到验证。

Conclusion: 通过分解工具发现，可以更细致地评估模型能力，并揭示了识别能力随模型增大而下降的反直觉现象。

中文摘要：现有的工具使用基准报告复杂多步任务的单一成功概率。受认知科学思想的启发，我们将工具使用与工具发现区分开来，并将后者分解为好奇心（模型发现构建工具所需部分的能力）、识别（模型发现创建工具过程的能力）以及效率（模型在工具创建后使用工具的能力）。我们表明该框架可应用于现有发现任务，例如Voyager。此外，我们提供证据表明识别与模型大小呈反比缩放，并引入和分析了一类组合游戏来证明这一点。我们进一步在另一个旨在模拟真实世界任务的环境中观察到反比缩放。

Original abstract: Existing tool-use benchmarks report a single success rate for complex, multistep tasks. Inspired by ideas from cognitive science, we distinguish tool use from tool discovery and decompose the latter into curiosity (the model's ability to discover the parts needed to build the tool), recognition (the model's ability to discover the process of creating the tool), and efficiency (the model's use of the tool after creation). We show that this framework can be applied to existing discovery tasks, such as Voyager. In addition, we provide evidence that recognition inversely scales with model size, and we introduce and analyze a class of combinatorial games that demonstrates this. We further observe inverse scaling in a separate environment designed to emulate real-world tasks.

### [72] [Is Progressive Disclosure All You Need for Long-Context Agents?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17598)
*Yifeng He,Yinzhe Zhao,Jicheng Wang,Hao Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文首次对照研究了长文档问答中渐进式披露模式，发现单层渐进式披露在单本书上优势取决于智能体框架强弱，在多本书时优于原始文档导航，且深层路由不必要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长文档问答面临上下文窗口限制与检索器选择的权衡，Agent Skills的渐进式披露被广泛采用但缺乏系统验证文献。

Method: 在InfiniteBench上，跨三个智能体框架和三个模型家族，对比原始文档导航、多种Agent Skills包设计与经典混合检索器的效果。

Result: 单本书时，增益依赖智能体框架，强框架下增益近零；多本书时，原始文档导航崩溃，单层渐进式披露表现更好，第二层路由无益甚至有害。

Conclusion: 渐进式披露通过节省上下文空间而非提升智能体能力起作用，在语料库过大时是关键，强智能体下则冗余，且一层即可。

中文摘要：长文档问答通常迫使我们做出选择：是将整个文档加载到上下文窗口中，还是额外添加一个独立的检索器。智能体人工智能提出了一种更广泛的选择：为智能体提供文档路径，让它自行决定如何阅读以及阅读什么。智能体技能（Agent Skills）是一种将专业知识打包成文件夹的标准，智能体可按需加载，它提供了一种现成的机制：渐进式披露，即仅暴露查询所需的内容，从简短描述到具体段落。从业者迅速将这种模式应用于书籍长度的理解任务，但支持这些选择的证据一直是传闻。我们首次对该模式进行了受控研究，在InfiniteBench上，跨三个智能体框架和三个模型家族，将原始文档导航和多种智能体技能包设计与经典的混合检索器进行比较。在单本书上，增益取决于智能体框架：当智能体对原始文档的导航能力较差时，增益较大；而当强大的智能体框架已经能够自行分割和检索时，增益近乎为零。当扩展到跨多本书的任务时，原始文档导航性能崩溃，而单层渐进式披露退化得更慢并取得领先。第二层更深的路由层从未有帮助，有时还会直接破坏准确性，因此单层就足够了。渐进式披露赢得的是上下文，而非智能：当强大的智能体能够自行定位正确段落时，它是冗余的；而当语料库变得过大无法通过阅读来导航时，它则至关重要。

Original abstract: Long-document question answering usually forces a choice between loading the whole document into the context window and bolting on a separate retriever. Agentic AI suggests a broader option, giving the agent the document path and letting it decide how and what to read. Agent Skills, a standard for packaging expertise into folders an agent loads on demand, supply a ready mechanism: progressive disclosure, which exposes only what a query needs, from a short description down to the specific passages. Practitioners rapidly adopted this pattern for book-length understanding tasks, but the evidence to support such choices has been anecdotal. We run the first controlled study of the pattern, comparing raw-document navigation and several designs of Agent Skills packs against a classical hybrid retriever across three agent harnesses and three model families on InfiniteBench. On a single book, the gain depends on the harness, running large when the agent navigates the raw document poorly but near zero when a strong agent harness already divides and retrieves on its own. When scaling up to tasks that span many books, raw-document navigation collapses while one-level progressive disclosure degrades more slowly and pulls ahead. A second, deeper routing level never helps and sometimes breaks accuracy outright, so one level is enough. Progressive disclosure buys context, not intelligence: it is redundant while a strong agent can locate the right passages itself, and decisive once the corpus grows too large to navigate by reading.

</details>


### [73] [Verify, Repair, Repeat, or Stop? Robust Stopping for Noisy Verify-Repair Loops in LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17641)
*Yitao Wu,Si Shen,Rui Yang,Hong Peng,Bin Hu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出VRR-Stop框架，通过噪声模型和信念过滤在验证-修复循环中实现鲁棒的停止决策，并在GSM8K上显著提升真实有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有验证-修复循环在噪声环境下缺乏原则性的停止标准，导致修复可能损害正确计划且真实有效性下降。

Method: 提出四参数噪声模型分离验证器错误和修复器行为，利用信念过滤估计有效性，基于边际增益符号决定停止，并结合无估计回退机制VRR-Guard应对验证器辨别力不足的情况。

Result: 在GSM8K压力测试中，VRR-Stop以平均0.72轮修复成本将最终真实有效性比固定五轮修复提高60.6个百分点。

Conclusion: 停止可靠性由验证器辨别力和决策裕度共同决定，而非估计误差的绝对大小。

中文摘要：验证-修复循环是大语言模型（LLM）代理在代码生成、数学推理和工具使用中纠正错误规划的标准手段。当验证器和修复器都存在噪声时，修复可能损害已经正确的规划，并且报告的接受率持续上升而真实有效性下降，因此现有方法缺乏决定何时停止修复的原则性基础。我们提出了VRR-Stop，一个针对含噪验证-修复-重复（VRR）循环的鲁棒停止框架。一个四参数噪声模型将验证器的错误接受和错误拒绝与修复器的修复和损害行为分开。信念过滤将重复的验证投票转化为对已承诺有效性的估计，循环根据真实边际增益的符号进行承诺或修复，这仅需要符号可识别性而非所有参数的准确恢复。当验证器辨别力接近零时，校准本身失败，估计误差可能翻转停止符号，因此我们将VRR-Stop与VRR-Guard配对，这是一种无估计的回退机制，仅在足够的验证裕度下替换当前的候选方案。在GSM8K压力测试中，VRR-Stop在平均0.72轮修复成本下，将最终真实有效性比固定五轮修复提高了60.6个百分点。在各种设置下，停止可靠性由验证器辨别力和决策裕度共同决定，而不是由估计误差的绝对大小决定。

Original abstract: Verify-repair loops are a standard means for large language model (LLM) agents to correct faulty plans in code generation, mathematical reasoning, and tool use. When both the verifier and the repairer are noisy, repair can damage already-correct plans, and reported acceptance keeps rising while true validity falls, so existing methods lack a principled basis for deciding when repair should stop. We propose VRR-Stop, a robust stopping framework for noisy verify-repair-repeat (VRR) loops. A four-parameter noise model separates verifier false acceptance and false rejection from the repair and damage behavior of the repairer. Belief filtering turns repeated verification votes into an estimate of committed validity, and the loop commits or repairs according to the sign of the true marginal gain, which requires only sign identifiability rather than accurate recovery of all parameters. When verifier discrimination approaches zero, calibration itself fails and estimation error can flip the stopping sign, so we pair VRR-Stop with VRR-Guard, an estimation-free fallback that replaces the incumbent candidate only under a sufficient verification margin. On a GSM8K stress setting, VRR-Stop improves final true validity by 60.6 percentage points over fixed five-round repair at an average cost of 0.72 repair rounds. Across settings, stopping reliability is governed jointly by verifier discrimination and the decision margin rather than by the absolute size of estimation error.

</details>


### [74] [Expected Free Energy as Belief-Dependent Utility for rho-POMDPs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16981)
*Patrick Cooper,Alvaro Velasquez*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 将预期自由能作为POMDP效用，为agent探索-利用权衡提供理论框架，可迁移。

TL;DR: 主动推理中的最小化期望自由能等价于一个具有固定探索权重（w=1）的ρ-POMDP，从而无需手动调整探索与利用的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准POMDP忽略信息的直接价值，而ρ-POMDP需要手动调整探索权重和效用函数，缺乏普适性。

Method: 通过证明最小化期望自由能与求解特定ρ-POMDP的等价性，将探索权重固定为1，并扩展到因子观测POMDP。

Result: 在多个环境中（Tiger、RockSample、新结构检测基准），未经调整的探索权重匹配或超越仅奖励规划，避免过度探索，并接近帕累托最优。

Conclusion: 主动推理提供了一种开箱即用的探索目标，适用于测试有成本的现实场景如故障检测和医疗筛查。

中文摘要：在部分可观测性下行动的智能体必须决定何时收集信息以及哪些观测值值得其成本。标准POMDP仅通过信息对奖励的最终影响来评估信息。相反，ρ-POMDP框架通过依赖于信念的效用ρ直接奖励不确定性减少，但在实践中，ρ的选择和其权重都需要针对每个任务手动调整。我们表明主动推理完全消除了这种调整。最小化期望自由能（EFE）完全等同于求解一个效用为期望信息增益的ρ-POMDP，并且探索权重固定为w=1，因为变分界以相同单位（纳特）表达了实用价值和认知价值。我们针对“先观察后承诺”POMDP证明了这一等价性，并将其扩展到因子观测POMDP，这是一个更广泛的类别，涵盖了交错观察-行动问题，例如无损检测和移动感知，其中信息收集保持隐藏状态不变。实验支持了该理论。在从经典Tiger问题到RockSample以及拥有超过65,000个状态的新结构检测基准测试中，未经调整的权重在相同规划范围内匹配或超越了仅奖励规划，避免了针对每个任务调整的奖励探勘中的过度探索，并位于成功-奖励帕累托前沿中最大化奖励的膝点附近。实际的收益是一个开箱即用的探索目标。在诸如故障检测和医疗筛查等应用中，每项测试都有价格，每个遗漏的故障都有成本，EFE提供了一种推导出来的而非调整的依赖于信念的效用。

Original abstract: An agent acting under partial observability must decide when to gather information and which observations are worth their cost. Standard POMDPs value information only through its eventual effect on reward. The $ρ$-POMDP framework instead rewards uncertainty reduction directly, through a belief-dependent utility $ρ$, but in practice both the choice of $ρ$ and the weight placed on it are tuned by hand for every task. We show that active inference removes this tuning entirely. Minimizing Expected Free Energy (EFE) is exactly equivalent to solving a $ρ$-POMDP whose utility is expected information gain, and the exploration weight is fixed at $w=1$ because the variational bound expresses pragmatic and epistemic value in the same units (nats). We prove this equivalence for observe-then-commit POMDPs and extend it to factored observation POMDPs, a broader class that covers interleaved observe-act problems such as non-destructive testing and mobile sensing, where gathering information leaves the hidden state unchanged. Experiments support the theory. Across environments ranging from the classic Tiger problem to RockSample and a new Structural Inspection benchmark with over 65,000 states, the untuned weight matches or outperforms reward-only planning at the same horizon, avoids the over-exploration of bonuses tuned per task, and sits near the reward-maximizing knee of the success-reward Pareto frontier. The practical payoff is an exploration objective that works out of the box. In applications such as fault detection and medical screening, where every test has a price and every missed fault has a cost, EFE supplies a belief-dependent utility that is derived rather than tuned.

</details>


### [75] [Reward-Driven LLM Agent Workflows: Synthesizing POMDP Routing and Self-Correction for Autonomous Decision-Making](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17038)
*Amez Amanj Ali,Kuo-Kun Tseng*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出奖励驱动的LLM agent工作流，包含POMDP路由和自我纠正，直接适用于agent规划与执行。

TL;DR: 提出一种基于POMDP路由和自纠正奖励模型的LLM智能体架构，在ALFWorld和WebShop上任务成功率绝对提升24.5%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决LLM智能体在长周期规划、稀疏奖励和动态环境交互中的挑战，克服传统静态提示方法的局限性。

Method: 引入POMDP路由机制，结合内部自纠正奖励模型，集成多模态输入和强化学习（PPO、值函数近似），维持长期记忆并动态调整推理路径。

Result: 在ALFWorld和WebShop上任务成功率和轨迹效率绝对提升24.5%，消融实验证实奖励驱动的批评模块显著抑制幻觉率。

Conclusion: 提供了可扩展的自主智能体框架，桥接强化学习和图记忆理论，适用于复杂多步自主系统。

中文摘要：该论文解决了当前大语言模型（LLM）智能体应用中的关键技术挑战，包括长周期规划、稀疏奖励归因和动态环境交互，通过设计和优化一个智能体工作流。提出的架构基于核心AI范式的综合：视觉、语言、生成、图、多模态、强化和智能体智能。与依赖静态提示且缺乏鲁棒感知-行动循环的传统基线模型不同，我们的方法引入了一个部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP）路由机制。该机制通过一个内部的、自纠正的奖励模型进行增强，该模型在执行前评估决策轨迹。通过整合多模态输入和先进的强化学习原理（如近端策略优化和值函数逼近），智能体保持长期结构记忆并动态调整其推理路径以减少错误累积。在ALFWorld具身仿真环境和WebShop在线导航基准上的实验表明，与主流基线（如标准ReAct框架）相比，任务成功率和轨迹效率绝对提升了24.5%。全面的消融研究证实了奖励驱动的批评模块在抑制幻觉率方面的显著贡献。本研究将强化学习和基于图的记忆的理论基础与自主智能体工作流相连接。最终，该架构为开发复杂多步自主系统中的人工智能技术提供了一个实用、可扩展的参考框架。代码可在https://github.com/01Amez/RLAW_Implementation获取。

Original abstract: This paper addresses key technical challenges in current large language model (LLM) agent applications, including long-horizon planning, sparse reward attribution, and dynamic environmental interaction, by designing and optimizing an intelligent agent workflow. The proposed architecture is based on the synthesis of core AI paradigms: Visual, Language, Generative, Graph, Multimodal, Reinforcement, and Agent Intelligence. Unlike conventional baseline models that rely on static prompting and lack robust perception-action loops, our approach introduces a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP) routing mechanism. This mechanism is augmented with an internal, self-correcting reward model that evaluates decision trajectories before execution. By integrating multimodal inputs and advanced reinforcement learning principles (such as proximal policy optimization and value function approximation), the agent maintains long-term structural memory and dynamically adapts its reasoning pathways to mitigate error accumulation. Empirical experiments on the ALFWorld embodied simulation environment and the WebShop online navigation benchmark demonstrate a 24.5% absolute improvement in task success rate and trajectory efficiency over mainstream baselines like the standard ReAct framework. Comprehensive ablation studies confirm the significant contribution of the reward-driven critique module in suppressing hallucination rates. This research bridges theoretical foundations of reinforcement learning and graph-based memory with autonomous agent workflows. Ultimately, the resulting architecture offers a practical, scalable reference framework for developing artificial intelligence technologies in complex, multi-step autonomous systems. Code is available at https://github.com/01Amez/RLAW_Implementation.

### [76] [When LLMs Over-Answer: Measuring and Mitigating Quality Issues in LLM-Based Hardware Description Language Question Answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17063)
*Ziteng Hu,Jiachi Chen,Wenhao Lv,Huan Zhang,Yingjie Xia*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 针对硬件描述语言QA，提出多agent框架改善回答质量，可迁移至代码优化agent的冗余与冗长问题。

TL;DR: LLM在HDL问答中存在过度回答倾向，即提供正确但冗余和冗长的答案；提出的多智能体框架可提高回答质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 调查LLM生成的HDL回答质量（与人类专家相比），并解决其过度回答（冗余和冗长）问题。

Method: 收集6,246个HDL问答帖子构建数据集；设计包含19名工程师的用户研究；提出多智能体框架，使用LLM-as-Judge和结构指标评估。

Result: LLM答案65.7%冗余、69.1%冗长，49%与专家答案不一致，但58.3%用户偏好其可读性；框架将核心答案质量从3.71提至4.67，非核心内容质量从3.72提至4.23。

Conclusion: 多智能体框架有效改善了LLM在HDL问答中的冗余和冗长问题，提升了答案质量。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）的快速发展导致从业者越来越依赖它们来回答关于硬件描述语言（HDL）的问题。由于HDL最终会被综合成物理硬件，一个不精确或冗余的回答可能会传播到时序违规或不可综合的逻辑中，这些问题在设计流程的后期才会显现，从而使HDL答案的质量尤为重要。然而，LLM生成的回答质量，特别是与人类专家提供的答案相比，尚不清楚。为了探究这一问题，我们从Stack Overflow收集了6,246个HDL问答帖子及其被接受的答案，并将其整理成一个数据集，按四个主要类别（概念、调试、生成和优化）和十个子类别进行分类。利用该数据集，我们设计了一项用户研究，参与者为19名具有一到三年经验的HDL工程师。我们的研究结果揭示了一种普遍存在的过度回答倾向：LLM提供了正确的内容，但将其埋藏在冗余的替代方案（65.7%）和冗长的填充（69.1%）之下，而近一半的答案（49.0%）未能完全与专家答案对齐，但参与者仍然更喜欢LLM回答的可读性（58.3%）。基于这些发现，我们提出了一个用于改进基于LLM的HDL问答的多智能体框架。我们使用LLM作为评判者以及两个结构指标来评估答案质量：核心答案数量（反映冗余，因为LLM经常提供多个替代解决方案）和非核心内容长度（反映冗长）。在四个主流LLM上评估，我们的框架将核心答案质量的平均得分从3.71提高到4.67（+0.96），非核心内容质量从3.72提高到4.23（+0.51），采用五分制。

Original abstract: The rapid advancement of large language models (LLMs) has led practitioners to increasingly rely on them for answering questions about hardware description languages (HDLs). Because HDL is ultimately synthesized into physical hardware, an imprecise or redundant answer can propagate into timing violations or non-synthesizable logic that surface only late in the design flow, making the quality of HDL answers especially consequential. However, the quality of LLM-generated responses, particularly in comparison with answers provided by human experts, remains unclear. To investigate this question, we collect 6,246 HDL Q&A posts with accepted answers from Stack Overflow and curate them into a dataset, organized into a taxonomy of four main categories (Conceptual, Debugging, Generation, and Optimization) and ten subcategories. Using this dataset, we design a user study conducted with 19 HDL engineers with one to three years of experience. Our findings reveal a pervasive over answering tendency: LLMs supply correct content but bury it under redundant alternatives (65.7%) and verbose padding (69.1%), while nearly half of answers (49.0%) fail to fully align with expert answers yet participants still preferred LLM responses for readability (58.3%). Motivated by these findings, we propose a multi-agent framework for improving LLM-based HDL question answering. We evaluate answer quality using an LLM-as-Judge and two structural metrics: the number of core answers, which reflects redundancy since LLMs often provide multiple alternative solutions, and the length of non-core content, which reflects verbosity. Evaluated on the four mainstream LLMs, our framework increases the average core-answer quality score from 3.71 to 4.67 (+0.96) and the non-core content quality from 3.72 to 4.23 (+0.51), on a five-point scale.

### [77] [Otap:Structure-Aware Optimal Transport for Evaluating Planning and Execution in Agent Trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17082)
*Babak Barazandeh,Subhabrata Majumdar,George Michailidis*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出基于最优传输的agent轨迹评估指标，直接用于评测agent规划与执行。

TL;DR: 提出一种基于最优传输的轨迹评估方法OTAP，通过计算执行图与有效解图间的距离来评估智能体规划，对依赖保持的重新排序鲁棒，能处理冗余和缺失步骤。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有二元成功标志无法区分合理与运气解决方案，且不解释失败原因；精确匹配惩罚有效但重新排序或不同分解的计划。

Method: 将轨迹评估重定义为执行图与有效解图间的距离，通过非平衡融合Gromov-Wasserstein最优传输在属性依赖图上实现。

Result: 在受控扰动和三个基准上，OTAP能在语义度量低于随机时区分有效和无效轨迹，准确率在依赖图精确时最高，启发式推断时下降。

Conclusion: OTAP是一个有效的伪度量，对依赖保持的重排序不变，对冗余步骤有界敏感，能处理缺失和幻觉步骤，适应粒度的变化。

中文摘要：大型语言模型代理通过生成交织了规划、工具调用和中间结果的轨迹来解决问题。当前的评估指标要么将这样的轨迹简化为一个二元成功标志，要么通过精确匹配将其与参考进行比较。成功标志无法区分合理的解决方案与凭运气成功的解决方案，并且对于失败运行出错的原因没有任何说明。精确匹配会惩罚那些有效但重新排序或分解方式与参考不同的计划。我们重新将轨迹评估定义为代理的执行图与一组有效解图之间的距离，并通过在属性依赖图上解决一个非平衡融合Gromov-Wasserstein最优传输问题来实例化它。得到的分数称为OTAP（用于智能体规划的最优传输），是一个伪度量，可证明对依赖保持的重新排序不变，并且对冗余步骤具有有界敏感性。其非平衡边际处理缺失或幻觉步骤而不强制匹配，其软耦合适应规划粒度的变化。在受控扰动和三个公开基准上，OTAP在语义度量得分低于随机水平的区域中区分有效和无效轨迹。其准确性在依赖图被准确恢复时最高，仅在从自由文本轨迹启发式推断图时下降。

Original abstract: Large language model agents solve tasks by generating trajectories that interleave planning, tool calls, and intermediate results. Current evaluation metrics reduce such a trajectory to a binary success flag or compare it against a reference by exact matching. A success flag cannot distinguish a sound solution from one that succeeds by luck, and says nothing about why a failed run went wrong. Exact matching penalizes plans that are valid but reordered or decomposed differently from the reference. We reframe trajectory evaluation as a distance between the agent's execution graph and a set of valid solution graphs, and instantiate it via an unbalanced fused Gromov-Wasserstein transport problem over attributed dependency graphs. The resulting score, termed \otap{} (Optimal Transport for Agentic Planning), is a pseudo-metric that is provably invariant to dependency-preserving reorderings and has bounded sensitivity to redundant steps. Its unbalanced marginals handle missing or hallucinated steps without forcing a match, and its soft coupling accommodates variation in plan granularity. On controlled perturbations and three public benchmarks, \otap{} separates valid from invalid trajectories in a regime where semantics-only metrics score below chance. Its accuracy is highest when the dependency graph is recovered exactly, and drops only when the graph is inferred heuristically from free-text traces.

### [78] [Evidence Interfaces Shape How Retrieval-Augmented Readers Use Support](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17108)
*Junchi Liao,Jiawen Deng,Fuji Ren*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究检索增强阅读器的证据接口，对RAG agent的上下文使用有启发。

TL;DR: 多跳RAG评估中，top-k分数掩盖支撑缺失和接口问题；使用支撑标注区分失败，发现短窗口在支撑完整时有效，支撑监督排序器提升覆盖并降低成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示top-k答案分数在多跳RAG评估中未能区分支撑缺失和接口不匹配的问题，提出更精细的评估方式。

Method: 使用三个支撑标注的多跳QA基准，比较原始上下文、检索窗口和黄金支持诊断渲染训练的匹配读者，并通过支撑移除检查分析收益来源。

Result: 短排名窗口在支撑完整时可匹配或改进原始上下文；支撑监督排序器提高覆盖率并恢复质量，收益依赖于暴露的证据。

Conclusion: 在支撑标注的评估中，top-k答案分数应与完整支撑覆盖率一起报告。

中文摘要：在多跳RAG评估中，top-k答案分数可能隐藏两种不同的失败：检索窗口可能丢失部分支撑链，或者它包含的支撑形式不适应经过调整的读者。我们将这种读者面临的证据形式称为证据接口。使用三个带有支撑标注的多跳QA基准，我们比较了使用原始上下文、检索窗口和黄金支持诊断渲染训练的匹配调整读者。这些比较区分了支撑可用性失败和剩余的读者接口效应。Top-k窗口仅在检查完整标注的支撑链是否存活时才变得可解释：当它存活时，短排名窗口可以匹配或改进原始上下文；当它不存活时，缺失的支撑解释了大部分损失。黄金支持优先改进了匹配读者；在2Wiki和MuSiQue上，支撑监督的排序器提高了覆盖率，并以更低的提示成本恢复了原始上下文的质量，同时保留了黄金提升空间。支撑移除检查进一步表明，收益依赖于暴露的证据，而不仅仅是答案先验。在支撑标注的评估中，top-k答案分数因此应与完整支撑覆盖率一起报告。

Original abstract: In multi-hop RAG evaluation, a top-k answer score can hide two different failures: the retrieval window may drop part of the support chain, or it may contain support in a form the adapted reader does not use well. We call this reader-facing form of retrieved evidence an evidence interface. Using three support-annotated multi-hop QA benchmarks, we compare matched adapted readers trained with raw context, retrieval windows, and gold-support diagnostic renderings. These comparisons distinguish support-availability failures from remaining reader-interface effects. Top-k windows become interpretable only after checking whether the complete annotated support chain survives: when it does, short ranked windows can match or improve over raw context; when it does not, missing support explains much of the loss. Gold support-first improves matched readers; on 2Wiki and MuSiQue, a support-supervised ranker raises coverage and recovers raw-context quality at lower prompt cost, while retaining gold headroom. Support-removal checks further show that the gains rely on exposed evidence, not only answer priors. On support-annotated evaluations, top-k answer scores should therefore be reported together with complete-support coverage.

### [79] [A Diagnostic Framework for AI Agent Behavior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17149)
*Xichen Zhang,Yingjie Zhang,Tianshu Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出AI agent行为诊断框架，从计算层和行为调制层归因，通用方法论。

TL;DR: 提出层归因框架，将AI行为归因于计算层和调制层，强调行为诊断需先确定来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI智能体越来越深度参与社会系统，但现有评估方法无法区分行为是源于智能体自身表征还是系统角色、规则等外部因素，导致治理和解释存在误判。

Method: 提出层归因框架，将行为分析分为基础计算层（架构、记忆等决定可能性）和行为调制层（身份、目标等塑造表达），结合案例说明框架应用。

Result: 框架揭示了三个关键后果：替代有效性依赖模型-任务-层关系；人机行为差异提供诊断线索；治理需在干预前进行源归因。

Conclusion: 将AI视为行为行动者需要先定位行为来源，再决定如何解释、验证或治理，而非直接观察表面行为。

中文摘要：AI智能体越来越多地在行为科学家研究的相同临床、政治、科学和社会系统中行动。评估这些系统需要源级诊断：相同的行为模式可能源于智能体的表征基底，也可能源于塑造其表达的角色、目标、互动结构和治理规则。本视角提出了一个用于AI智能体行为的诊断框架：层归因。基础计算层通过架构、记忆、感知、注意和表征定义了哪些行为是可能的。行为调制层通过身份、资源、目标、社会互动、制度约束和治理塑造了这些能力如何表达。该框架阐明了三个后果：替代有效性是一种模型-任务-层关系，人机差异提供了诊断证据，治理需要在干预前进行源归因。因此，将AI智能体视为行为行动者需要评估方法，在决定如何解释、验证或治理行为之前确定行为源于何处。

Original abstract: AI agents increasingly act within the same clinical, political, scientific, and social systems that behavioral scientists study. Evaluating these systems requires source-level diagnosis: the same behavioral pattern may arise from an agent representational substrate or from the roles, objectives, interaction structures, and governance rules that shape its expression. This Perspective proposes a diagnostic framework for AI agent behavior: layer attribution. The foundational computational layer defines what behaviors are possible through architecture, memory, perception, attention, and representation. The behavioral modulation layer shapes how those capacities are expressed through identity, resources, objectives, social interaction, institutional constraints, and governance. The framework clarifies three consequences: surrogate validity is a model-task-layer relation, human-AI divergence provides diagnostic evidence, and governance requires source attribution before intervention. Treating AI agents as behavioral actors therefore requires evaluation methods that determine where behavior originates before deciding how to explain, validate, or govern it.

### [80] [Is Your Model Thinking or Just Stagnating? PUMA: Diagnosing Reasoning Pathology via Phase-Momentum Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17188)
*Cheng Yan,Guangyang Ye,Wuyang Zhang,Fan Xu,Zhijun Fan,Xiang Xia,Yanyong Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 诊断推理模型过度思考问题，对agent推理效率优化有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 提出PUMA框架，通过相位-动量对齐解决LRM的过度思考，提升测试时效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有测试时效率优化方法在动态推理中实时性不足，信息论方法易受欺骗性收敛，潜在表示分析缺乏实时敏感性。

Method: 提出相位-动量对齐假说和认知能量模型，基于此设计无训练框架PUMA，包含分层诊断架构，结合轻量相位监测与事件触发几何分析，实现自适应截断或纠正。

Result: 在1.5B到32B的LRMs上，PUMA在多个基准测试中优于最先进基线，实现更优的准确率-效率权衡和稳健跨领域泛化。

Conclusion: PUMA有效提升LRM测试时效率，区分主动探索与被动停滞，具有良好泛化能力。

中文摘要：测试时缩放使大型推理模型（LRMs）能够通过广泛的思维链（CoT）处理复杂任务。然而，这常常引发“过度思考”悖论，即冗余推理增加计算开销而不保证准确性。现有的测试时效率优化方法主要分为两类：信息论方法，容易陷入“欺骗性收敛”，即低不确定性掩盖幻觉；以及潜在表示分析，通常事后进行，缺乏动态推理所需的实时敏感性。为弥补这一差距，我们首先提出相位-动量对齐假说，断言推理正确性取决于几何动量与不确定性解决之间的时间同步。然后我们理论上构建认知能量模型，通过两个正交维度表征这些动态：几何认知努力（由潜在速度和曲折度量化）和熵认知不确定性。为实施这一模型，我们引入PUMA（相位-不确定性动量对齐），一个无训练框架，采用分层诊断架构。通过将轻量级相位监测与事件触发的几何分析相结合，PUMA有效区分主动探索和被动停滞，通过自适应截断或纠正措施实现精确干预。在从1.5B到32B的LRMs上的大量实验表明，PUMA在各种基准测试中始终优于最先进的基线，实现了优越的准确率-效率权衡和稳健的跨领域泛化。

Original abstract: Test-time scaling empowers Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) to tackle complex tasks via extensive Chain-of-Thought (CoT). However, this often induces the "overthinking" paradox, where redundant reasoning increases computational overhead without guaranteeing accuracy. Existing test-time efficiency optimization methods primarily fall into two categories: information-theoretic approaches, which are prone to "deceptive convergence" where low uncertainty masks hallucinations, and latent representation analyses, which are often post-hoc, lacking the real-time sensitivity for dynamic reasoning. To bridge this gap, we first posit the Phase-Momentum Alignment Hypothesis, asserting that reasoning correctness hinges on the temporal synchronization between geometric momentum and uncertainty resolution. We then theoretically formulate the Cognitive-Energy Model to characterize these dynamics through two orthogonal dimensions: Geometric Cognitive Effort, quantified by latent velocity and tortuosity, and Entropic Cognitive Uncertainty. To operationalize this, we introduce PUMA (Phase-Uncertainty Momentum Alignment), a training-free framework employing a tiered diagnostic architecture. By coupling lightweight phase monitoring with event-triggered geometric analysis, PUMA effectively distinguishes active exploration from passive stagnation, enabling precise interventions through adaptive truncation or corrective measures. Extensive experiments on LRMs spanning 1.5B to 32B demonstrate that PUMA consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines across diverse benchmarks, achieving a superior accuracy-efficiency trade-off and robust cross-domain generalization.

### [81] [Toward Anthropomorphic Dialogue: A Closed-Loop Framework for Human-Like Chat Generation, Evaluation, and Preference Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17191)
*Wentao Liu,Siyu Song,Xi Chen,Youjia Li,Xiaokun Wang,Min Ji,Ji Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出拟人对话agent框架，包含评估与偏好对齐，属于通用agent对准方法。

TL;DR: 提出AnthroDial框架，通过联合系统架构、可执行评估和诊断对齐的闭环方法，显著提升拟人化对话的严格准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对话系统仅关注流畅性，缺乏对个性、关系、记忆等拟人化要素的建模，导致无法实现类人私聊。

Method: 设计角色调度运行时、多维可执行基准，以及基于认知诊断和ZPD感知奖励的GRPO后训练流水线。

Result: Qwen3.6-27B-SFT+RL达到39.00%严格准确率和98.5总分；9B非思考设置中SFT和RL分别提升13.00%和18.37%严格准确率。

Conclusion: 生成、评估和奖励塑造共享行为维度能有效提升拟人化对话性能。

中文摘要：类人私聊需要的不仅仅是流畅的回复生成：系统必须保持个性、关系、记忆、有限知识、媒介特定的时机以及连贯的多轮对话弧。我们提出AnthroDial，一个闭环框架，将拟人化对话表述为系统架构、可执行评估和诊断对齐的联合问题。它结合了（1）一个基于角色调度的对话运行时，包含个性和场景卡片、长期记忆、虚拟时间和单稿消息决策；（2）一个可执行基准，包含L0有效性门控、五个每轮维度和五个对话级维度；（3）一个后训练流水线，过滤出16,436个调度决策示例用于SFT，并应用带有认知诊断和ZPD感知奖励的GRPO。该奖励维护每个行为维度的卡尔曼滤波能力估计，对能力缺陷较大的维度赋予更高权重，并使用rollout分数作为任务级ZPD匹配，以聚焦于可学习的薄弱技能。在包含55个个性、50个场景、50个个性-场景绑定以及每个模型100个角色条件案例的基准上，我们评估了16个系统，涵盖前沿基线、开放模型、思考/非思考变体以及SFT/RL消融实验。最强的非训练基线达到了32.00%的严格准确率，而Qwen3.6-27B-SFT+RL达到了39.00%的严格准确率和98.5的总分。在9B非思考设置中，SFT和RL将严格准确率从0.00%提高到13.00%和18.37%。这些结果表明，当生成、评估和奖励塑造共享相同的行为维度时，拟人化对话会受益。

Original abstract: Human-like private chat requires more than fluent response generation: a system must preserve persona, relationship, memory, bounded knowledge, medium-specific timing, and a coherent multi-turn arc. We present AnthroDial, a closed-loop framework that formulates anthropomorphic dialogue as a joint problem of system architecture, executable evaluation, and diagnostic alignment. It combines (1) a role-conditioned scheduled dialogue runtime with persona and scenario cards, long-term memory, virtual time, and single-draft message decisions; (2) an executable benchmark with an L0 validity gate, five per-turn dimensions, and five dialogue-level dimensions; and (3) a post-training pipeline that filters 16,436 scheduled-decision examples for SFT and applies GRPO with a cognitive-diagnostic, ZPD-aware reward. The reward maintains Kalman-filtered capability estimates for each behavioral dimension, upweights dimensions with larger capability deficits, and uses rollout scores as task-level ZPD matches to focus optimization on learnable weak skills. On a benchmark with 55 personas, 50 scenarios, 50 persona-scenario bindings, and 100 role-conditioned cases per model, we evaluate 16 systems spanning frontier baselines, open models, thinking/no-think variants, and SFT/RL ablations. The strongest non-trained baseline reaches 32.00% strict ACC, while Qwen3.6-27B-SFT+RL reaches 39.00% strict ACC and a 98.5 overall score. In the 9B no-think setting, SFT and RL improve strict ACC from 0.00% to 13.00% and 18.37%. These results show that anthropomorphic dialogue benefits when generation, evaluation, and reward shaping share the same behavioral dimensions.

### [82] [Constrained Path Reasoning: Measuring When Committed Stages Earn Their Cost](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17240)
*Honglin Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出约束路径推理框架，用于LLM推理流水线的阶段代价分析，对agent规划中的承诺与回溯有启发。

TL;DR: 约束路径推理（CPR）评估LLM推理中承诺中间阶段的成本效益，通过残差分类和固定LLM核算等实验表明，在特定条件下可显著提高可用产量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究LLM推理管线中承诺的中间阶段在何种条件下能够证明其成本是值得的，即何时引入硬约束的收益超过其代价。

Method: 提出约束路径推理（CPR）框架，结合源感知路径假设与阶段级核算；使用搜索生成临时状态，区分硬约束和软提案；通过形式化涵盖离散和连续承诺，并测量有效分支、端点集中度和每可用输出成本；在QCQP实例和退化多项式实例上进行实验，包括残差分类、固定LLM核算、配对条件调用和端点探测。

Conclusion: 模型生成的状态提供假设，而可信执行（硬约束）赢得约束强度，即合理使用经过验证的不变量能够有效提升推理性能。

中文摘要：在LLM推理管线中，承诺的中间阶段何时能够证明其成本是值得的？约束路径推理（CPR）将源感知路径假设与阶段级核算相结合。搜索生成临时状态；可信或经过验证的不变量可以进行硬约束，而其他提案则保持软性和可修正性。CPR预测，任务兼容的承诺可以分解转换、集中候选质量、诱导规律性，并在其收益超过传播误差和执行成本时暴露反馈。该形式化涵盖离散承诺和连续流，并衡量有效分支、端点集中度以及每可用输出的成本。在1180个生成的QCQP和40个精心设计的退化多项式实例（2140个端点）中，残差分类恢复了修复全部方案额外可行产量的63.0%，仅用其17.7%的尝试。固定LLM核算（270个在嵌套分支间共享的唯一调用）发现直接可用产量为41.1%，形式化和确定性执行后为90.0%，一次性凸化后为20.0%，完整路径为21.1%。在120次配对条件调用中，两个动作的回滚规则达到90%的可用产量，而反馈条件选择器为36.7%。两个端点探测将来源与验证分开：一个72输出的跨轨迹移植降低了熵和可接受质量；一个24输出的同调用自我提议试点给出了不变的双重复碰撞熵，可用产量为25.0%对8.3%，以及1/8的确定性确认端点检查。模型生成的状态提供假设；可信执行赢得约束强度。

Original abstract: When does a committed intermediate stage in an LLM reasoning pipeline earn its cost? Constrained Path Reasoning (CPR) pairs a source-aware path hypothesis with stage-level accounting. Search generates provisional states; trusted or validated invariants can constrain hard, while other proposals remain soft and revisable. CPR predicts that task-compatible commitments can factor transitions, concentrate candidate mass, induce regularity, and expose feedback when their gains exceed propagated error and execution cost. The formalism covers discrete commitments and continuous flows and measures effective branching, endpoint concentration, and cost per usable output. Across 1,180 generated QCQPs and 40 engineered degenerate polynomial instances (2,140 endpoints), residual triage recovers 63.0% of repair-all's additional feasible yield with 17.7% of its attempts. Fixed-LLM accounting (270 unique calls shared across nested arms) finds usable yield of 41.1% direct, 90.0% after formalization and deterministic execution, 20.0% after one-shot convexification, and 21.1% for the full path. In 120 paired-condition calls, a two-action rollback rule reaches 90% usable yield versus 36.7% for the feedback-conditioned selector. Two endpoint probes separate source from validation: a 72-output cross-trajectory transplant reduces entropy and acceptable mass; a 24-output same-call self-proposal pilot gives unchanged two-repeat collision entropy, 25.0% versus 8.3% usable yield, and 1/8 deterministically confirmed endpoint checks. Model-generated states supply hypotheses; trusted execution earns constraint strength.

### [83] [LenGuard-GPC: Length Guarding with Guided-Prompt Consistency for Spatial Reasoning Reinforce Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17243)
*Xingjian Tao,Yiwei Wang,Yujun Cai,Jing Tang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出强化学习密集奖励框架，用于控制推理长度，可迁移至agent训练中的效率优化。

TL;DR: LenGuard-GPC通过基于KL散度的密集奖励和分段长度奖励，在多视图空间推理中提高了GRPO的准确率并减少了响应长度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的GRPO奖励稀疏，无法定位错误轨迹且无法控制推理长度，导致推理冗长且不准确。

Method: 提出LenGuard-GPC框架，通过比较标准提示和引导提示下的词元级预测分布计算KL散度作为密集奖励，并引入分段长度奖励来控制推理长度。

Result: 在六个多视图空间推理基准上，LenGuard-GPC提高了准确率并减少了平均响应长度，优于GRPO。

Conclusion: LenGuard-GPC有效地解决多视图空间推理中推理冗长和准确率低的问题。

中文摘要：多视图空间推理要求视觉语言模型比较跨图像的视觉证据、对齐物体对应关系，并在长视觉上下文中推断空间关系，在这种情况下，思维链推理往往会变得冗长而不会变得更准确。带有可验证奖励的强化学习自然适用于此任务，但标准的GRPO奖励依赖于稀疏的结果级反馈，既不提供推理轨迹出错位置的信号，也不控制其长度。我们提出了LenGuard-GPC，一个同时解决这两个问题的密集奖励框架。对于每个采样轨迹，它比较标准提示和引导提示下的词元级别预测分布，并使用由此产生的词元和KL散度作为密集奖励信号。由于这个KL惩罚在词元上累积，否则会奖励较短的响应而不考虑其质量，我们引入了分段长度奖励，将推理长度控制在合理范围内，而不仅仅是鼓励简洁性。在六个多视图空间推理基准上，LenGuard-GPC在降低平均响应长度的同时，提高了准确率，优于原始GRPO。

Original abstract: Multi-view spatial reasoning requires vision-language models to compare visual evidence across images, align object correspondences, and infer spatial relations over long visual contexts, a setting where chain-of-thought reasoning tends to grow verbose without becoming more accurate. Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards is a natural fit for this task, but standard GRPO reward relies on sparse outcome-level feedback and gives no signal about where a reasoning trajectory goes wrong, nor any control over its length. We propose LenGuard-GPC, a dense reward framework that addresses both problems together. For each sampled trajectory, it compares the token-wise predictive distributions under a standard prompt and a guided prompt, and uses the resulting token-sum KL divergence as a dense reward signal. Since this KL penalty accumulates over tokens and would otherwise reward shorter responses regardless of their quality, we introduce a staged length bonus that keeps reasoning length within a controlled range without simply encouraging brevity. On six multi-view spatial reasoning benchmarks, LenGuard-GPC improves accuracy over vanilla GRPO while reducing average response length.

中文摘要：大型语言模型在神经权重中隐式编码世界模型，这在高精度领域（如医学和金融）中暴露了四种结构性风险：幻觉、冻结知识、可解释性差和可修改性差。本文提出数据优先本体论：将大型语言模型视为推理和语言引擎，而将确定性知识移入显式多模态数据库DaoQL。我们形式化了显式世界模型，并证明在规则独立性、确定性评估和固定冲突解决下，显式模型为可组合反事实分解性提供了充分条件；隐式模型缺乏原子读/增量语义，因此无法提供可比较的架构保证。实现的系统专注于DaoQL的验证存储层和显式评估路径，在一个进程中集成了图、列、向量和全文引擎。KVCache图节点、专家热更新和DaoQL-Agent运行时仍是未来工作。在嵌入式同机设置中，DaoQL报告图BFS为1.20毫秒，HNSW为83.1微秒，Fluent混合查询为105.8微秒；这些结果表明工程潜力，但必须考虑与客户端-服务器系统的部署形态差异。在LDBC SNB SF1和ANN-Benchmarks上的探索性测量进一步显示，交互式类查询的查询覆盖率为34/34，大多在亚毫秒到毫秒范围内，但由于长尾BI/IC查询，整体QPS仅为1.8；在桥边保护修复后，ANN-Benchmarks在千级QPS下达到Recall@10 >= 99%。在五领域反事实实验（n=1250）中，DaoQL+GPT-4o实现了94%的可组合反事实分解性，比单独的GPT-4o高出49个百分点。本文明确区分了可证明结构、初步实证证据和架构路线图声明。

Original abstract: Large language models encode world models implicitly in neural weights, which exposes four structural risks in high-precision domains such as medicine and finance: hallucination, frozen knowledge, poor explainability, and poor modifiability. This paper proposes data-first ontology: LLMs are treated as reasoning and language engines, while deterministic knowledge is moved into an explicit multimodal database, DaoQL. We formalize an explicit world model and show that, under rule independence, deterministic evaluation, and fixed conflict resolution, explicit models provide a sufficient condition for composable counterfactual decomposability; implicit models lack atomic read/delta semantics and therefore provide no comparable architectural guarantee. The implemented system focuses on DaoQL's verified storage layer and explicit Eval path, integrating graph, column, vector, and full-text engines within one process. In a five-domain counterfactual experiment (n = 1250), DaoQL+GPT-4o achieves 94% composable counterfactual decomposability, 49 percentage points above GPT-4o alone. Original abstract: Enterprise Resource Planning (ERP) systems record transactions reliably but still delegate almost all operational decision-making to human specialists, because classical rule-based automation cannot reason about exceptions and monolithic AI assistants degrade when asked to coordinate across functional boundaries. The work shows that role-aligned LLM agents under human oversight can move an ERP system from passively recording transactions to actively executing operational decisions, and it provides a reference architecture and an evaluation protocol for autonomous enterprise resource planning.

### [86] [Self-Modifying Lean Proof Agents with Verifier-Grounded Benchmark Coevolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17352)
*Yuqing Li,Zeguan Wu,Yu Gan,Junyu Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自演化Lean证明agent，含验证循环与基准共演化，直接启发代码优化

TL;DR: 提出一种自我进化的Lean证明代理，通过共同进化代理和基准，在miniF2F上达到45.1%的求解率，显著优于固定基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Lean证明代理的工作流程大多由人工设计，缺乏自适应能力，而代码级自我进化代理的成功表明工作流程也可以进化。因此，研究如何自动进化证明工作流程以提升性能。

Method: 设计一个自我进化的Lean证明代理，包含固定可信运行时和可变工作空间；采用共同进化策略，同时进化代理和基准；通过掌握度阈值控制的课程更新和单锚定重新校准来调整任务难度和保持分数可比性；所有进化在Lean验证循环内进行。

Result: 在保留的miniF2F测试集上，最佳共同进化代理达到45.1%的求解率，远高于种子代理的12.7%和最佳固定基准代理的32.0%。

Conclusion: 验证器基础的自我进化能够有效改进Lean证明工作流程，特别是在共同进化基准下，性能提升显著，表明该方法具有潜力。

中文摘要：设计有效的Lean证明代理是形式化数学推理中的一个核心挑战。除了构建更强的证明器外，近期工作强调了围绕Lean的工作流程：代理如何分解证明义务、使用工具和编译器反馈、诊断失败、修复证明以及维护结构化的证明上下文。受代码级自我进化代理的启发，我们研究此类工作流程是否可以被进化而非手动设计。我们提出了一种自我进化的Lean证明代理，其中一个小型固定的、可信的运行时包装了一个完全可变的工作空间：证明工作流程、提示和工具。与大多数针对固定外部基准进行优化的自我进化系统不同，我们的系统共同进化代理及其基准。在代际之间，最高分的代理（冠军）通过掌握度阈值控制的课程更新来修改活跃任务分布，仅在当前水平掌握后才引入更难的证明义务，并且通过单锚定重新校准在更新后的基准上重新运行冠军，以保持分数在难度增加时具有可比性。所有进化都保持在Lean验证循环内：无论代理如何重写自身，只有当其行为在可信快照下产生Lean验证的证明时才算成功，并且每次尝试必须发出机器可读的、基于Lean的证明上下文，其表示形式可能进化但基础性得到强制执行。我们运行共同进化轨迹和固定基准基线共15个活跃代，并在一个保留的miniF2F测试拆分上进行比较。最佳共同进化代理达到45.1%的保留求解率，而种子为12.7%，最佳固定基准代理为32.0%，表明验证器基础的自我进化可以在共同进化基准下改进Lean证明工作流程。

Original abstract: Designing effective Lean proof agents is a central challenge in formal mathematical reasoning. Beyond building stronger provers, recent work emphasizes the workflow around Lean: how an agent decomposes proof obligations, uses tools and compiler feedback, diagnoses failures, repairs proofs, and maintains structured proof context. Motivated by code-level self-evolving agents, we study whether such workflows can be evolved rather than hand-designed. We present a self-evolving Lean proof agent in which a small fixed, trusted runtime wraps a fully mutable workspace: the proof workflow, prompts, and tools. Unlike most self-evolving systems, which optimize against a fixed external benchmark, our system coevolves the agent and its benchmark. Between generations, the highest-scoring agent (the champion) revises the active task distribution through a mastery-throttled curriculum update that introduces harder proof obligations only after the current level is mastered, and a single-anchor recalibration re-runs the champion on the updated benchmark to keep scores comparable as difficulty rises. All evolution stays inside a Lean-grounded verification loop: however the agent rewrites itself, a success counts only when its behavior yields Lean-verified proofs under a trusted snapshot, and each attempt must emit a machine-readable, Lean-grounded proof context whose representation may evolve but whose groundedness is enforced. We run the coevolving trajectory and a fixed-benchmark baseline for 15 active generations and compare them on a held-out miniF2F test split. The best coevolving agent reaches a 45.1% held-out solve rate, versus 12.7% for the seed and 32.0% for the best fixed-benchmark agent, showing that verifier-grounded self-evolution can improve Lean proof workflows under a coevolving benchmark.

</details>


### [87] [Intermittent Control Is Not Diluted Control: A Switching Effect in Artificial Agency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17432)
*Veronique Ziegler*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自适应agent间歇控制效应，通用控制时序原理

TL;DR: 在历史依赖的自适应代理中，间歇性预期控制可降低平均调节负担，且效果优于固定模式混合的预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验一个简单预期：代理在预期控制和反应性控制之间切换时的调节负担应等于两种固定模式的加权平均。

Method: 在具有保留状态历史的模拟自适应代理中，分别测试周期性切换和随机切换调度下的调节负担，每个调度运行1000个匹配副本进行高统计量分析。

Result: 发现负的非线性切换惩罚：间歇性预期控制下的平均调节负担低于固定模式混合预测值，效应约占平均增益的0.5%，63-68%的副本低于零，且无累积负担。

Conclusion: 时间顺序影响调节负担，间歇性预期控制可作为降低长期恢复负担的机制，具有设计相关性。

中文摘要：自适应代理并不总是在相同的时间条件下进行调节。有时稳定可以在干扰完全进入内部状态之前就开始；在其他时候，代理只能在干扰发生后恢复。一个简单的预期是，在这两种条件之间移动的代理应该表现得像两种固定情况的加权平均值：花在反应性恢复上的时间越多，调节负担越大。本文表明这种预期可能失败。在一个具有保留状态历史的模拟自适应代理中，在一个操作点上，持续的反应性控制比持续的预期控制成本更高，间歇性获得预期控制将平均调节负担降低到低于固定模式混合预测的值。这种效应在周期性和随机切换调度下都会出现：失去预期访问并不只是稀释其益处，而间歇性地恢复它可以重新组织后续的调节负担。高统计运行（每个调度N=1000个匹配副本）在每个测试调度下解析出负的非线性切换惩罚。效应虽小但一致：约占平均增益的0.5%，63-68%的副本低于零。晚期窗口诊断未发现未解决的调节负担累积。该结果确定了一个设计相关的时间原理。在历史依赖的自适应系统中，保持组织的负担不仅取决于代理在每个模式下花费的时间；干扰和恢复进入状态的顺序可以改变后续负担。因此，间歇性预期控制可能更像是一种降低长期恢复负担的机制，而不是调节的部分失败。

Original abstract: Adaptive agents do not always regulate under the same timing conditions. Sometimes stabilization can begin before a disturbance has fully entered the internal state; at other times the agent can only recover after disruption has taken hold. A simple expectation is that an agent moving between these conditions should behave like a weighted average of the two fixed cases: the more time spent in reactive recovery, the greater the regulatory burden.
  This paper shows that expectation can fail. In a simulated adaptive agent with retained state history, at an operating point where sustained reactive control is more costly than sustained anticipatory control, intermittent access to anticipatory control reduces the mean regulatory burden below the value predicted by a fixed-mode mixture. The effect appears under both periodic and stochastic switching schedules: losing anticipatory access does not simply dilute its benefit, and restoring it intermittently can reorganize the later regulatory burden. High-statistics runs (N = 1000 matched replicates per schedule) resolve a negative nonlinear switching penalty across every tested schedule. The effect is small but consistent: about half a percent of the mean gain, with 63-68% of replicates falling below zero. Late-window diagnostics reveal no unresolved upward accumulation of regulatory burden.
  The result identifies a design-relevant timing principle. In history-dependent adaptive systems, the burden of remaining organized is not set only by how much time an agent spends in each mode; the order in which disturbance and recovery enter the state can change the subsequent burden. Intermittent anticipatory control may therefore act less like a partial failure of regulation than like a mechanism for reducing the long-term burden of recovery.

</details>


### [88] [Empirical Grounding Improves the Realism of LLM Agents Simulating Human Behavior During Disruptions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17437)
*Chen Xia,Zexi Kuang,Yuqing Hu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM agent经验基础提高模拟真实性，可迁移至初始化方法

TL;DR: 经验依据能显著提升LLM智能体模拟人群行为的统计真实性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体模拟人类行为时存在有效性问题，个体合理推理无法复现人群行为，需要评估经验依据是否能改进。

Method: 开发了一个基于经验依据的LLM智能体框架，嵌入美国社区调查的人口统计、美国时间使用调查的日常活动及城市空间背景，并用2024年费城热浪期间的独立家庭调查作为外部验证基准。

Result: 与无依据基线相比，经验依据模型在正常和热浪条件下均显著提高了相关性（正常：0.528→0.912；热浪：0.349→0.836）并降低了均方误差（正常：0.066→0.008；热浪：0.098→0.012），热浪响应幅度捕捉率从20.6%提升至46.4%。

Conclusion: 经验依据使LLM智能体成为更可信的人群行为模拟器，但在建模人类适应能力方面仍有差距。

中文摘要：大语言模型（LLM）智能体提供了一种生成式方法来模拟人类行为，尤其是在可能没有或很少有直接历史相似情况的条件下的行为，这是灾害和基础设施中断规划中常见的挑战。然而，这种生成能力产生了一个有效性问题：个体上合理的智能体推理可能无法重现经验性的人群行为。我们评估了经验性依据是否提高了LLM智能体在中断期间模拟的统计真实性。具体来说，我们开发了一个基于经验依据的LLM智能体框架，该框架将美国社区调查的人口统计特征、美国时间使用调查的基线日常活动以及城市空间背景嵌入到智能体的初始化、记忆、决策提示和活动执行中。一项在2024年7月费城热浪期间进行的独立家庭调查被保留作为外部验证基准。与无依据的LLM智能体基线相比，基于经验依据的模型改进了对正常日常活动的重建，将平均相关性与经验活动分布从0.528提高到0.912，并将均方误差从0.066降低到0.008。在热浪条件下，基于经验依据的模型更好地再现了调查得出的活动分布，将平均相关性从0.349提高到0.836，并将均方误差从0.098降低到0.012。基于经验依据的模型捕捉到了观察到的热浪响应幅度的46.4%，而无依据基线仅为20.6%。这些发现表明，经验性依据可以使LLM智能体成为统计上更可信的人群行为模拟器，同时揭示了在建模人类适应能力方面仍存在的差距。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents offer a generative approach to simulating human behavior under conditions that may have few or no direct historical analogues, a common challenge in disaster and infrastructure-disruption planning. However, this generative capacity creates a validity problem: individually plausible agent reasoning may fail to reproduce empirical population behavior. We evaluate whether empirical grounding improves the statistical realism of LLM-agent simulations during disruptions. Specifically, we develop an empirically grounded LLM-agent framework that embeds demographic profiles from the American Community Survey, baseline routines from the American Time Use Survey, and urban spatial context into agent initialization, memory, decision prompts, and activity execution. An independent household survey conducted during the July 2024 Philadelphia heatwave is reserved as an external validation benchmark. Compared with an ungrounded LLM-agent baseline, the grounded model improved reconstruction of normal daily routines, increasing mean correlation with empirical activity profiles from 0.528 to 0.912 and reducing mean squared error from 0.066 to 0.008. Under heatwave conditions, the grounded model better reproduced survey-derived activity profiles, increasing mean correlation from 0.349 to 0.836 and reducing mean squared error from 0.098 to 0.012. The grounded model captured 46.4% of observed heatwave response amplitude, compared with 20.6% for the ungrounded baseline. These findings show that empirical grounding can make LLM agents more statistically credible simulators of population behavior while revealing remaining gaps in modeling human adaptation during disruptions.

### [89] [Can AI Agents Really Complete RTL-to-GDS? Lessons from Benchmarking Tool-Interactive EDA Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17528)
*Jinyuan Deng,Zhengrui Chen,Xufeng Wei,Tianyu Xing,Chenyi Wen,Cheng Zhuo*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: AI agent完成RTL-to-GDS流程，直接评估coding agent能力如同代码优化

TL;DR: FluxBench系统评估了AI代理在端到端EDA工作流中的性能，揭示了代理架构和基础模型能力的关键作用，并引入Token ROI效率指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估主要关注单个语言模型在孤立EDA任务上的表现，缺乏对不同代理系统在完整EDA流程中的性能洞察。

Method: 提出了FluxBench，一种在统一提示、工具环境和技术库设置下对AI代理在端到端EDA工作流上进行系统评估的方法，并引入Token ROI成本效率度量。

Result: 实验表明，基于相同基础模型的不同代理架构性能差距达86.27%，Token ROI差异高达105.92倍；在以PicoRV32为案例的RTL-to-GDS流程中，FluxEDA得分97.94，优于Claude Code 8.39倍。

Conclusion: 领域特定技能本身不足以在大规模EDA场景中提升代理性能，代理系统设计和基础模型能力共同在实现有效的自动化EDA工作流中起关键作用。

中文摘要：基于LLM的代理系统已成为电子设计自动化（EDA）领域的一种有前途的范式，显示出自动化复杂设计工作流的强大潜力。然而，现有的评估主要考察单个语言模型在孤立EDA任务上的表现，对不同代理系统在完整EDA流程中的性能提供的见解有限。在这项工作中，我们提出了FluxBench，一种在统一提示、工具环境和技术库设置下对AI代理在端到端EDA工作流上进行系统评估的方法。我们的评估涵盖了代表性场景，包括使用开源工具链的RTL生成以及使用闭源商业EDA工具进行工业应用的RTL-to-GDS流程。通过这些工作流，我们评估了代理在RTL代码生成、迭代修复、工具反馈利用、逻辑综合、布局布线（P&R）和工程变更订单（ECO）自动化方面的能力。为了进一步表征代理系统的效率，我们引入了Token ROI，一种成本效率度量，它衡量相对于令牌使用和运行时间成本的有效改进。实验结果表明，即使基于相同的基础模型，不同的代理系统架构也可能表现出高达86.27%的性能差距。此外，在任务性能相当的系统之间，Token ROI可能相差高达105.92倍。在以PicoRV32为案例的RTL-to-GDS流程中，FluxEDA的端到端得分高达97.94，优于配备领域特定EDA技能的Claude Code，最高可达8.39倍。这些结果表明，仅靠领域特定技能不足以在大规模EDA场景中提高代理性能。相反，代理系统设计和基础模型能力在实现有效的自动化EDA工作流中都发挥着关键作用。

Original abstract: LLM-driven agent systems have emerged as a promising paradigm for electronic design automation (EDA), demonstrating strong potential for automating complex design workflows. However, existing evaluations primarily examine individual language models on isolated EDA tasks, providing limited insight into how different agent systems perform across complete EDA flows. In this work, we present FluxBench, a systematic evaluation of AI agents on end-to-end EDA workflows under unified prompts, tool environments, and technology library settings. Our evaluation covers representative scenarios, including RTL generation with open-source toolchains and an RTL-to-GDS flow using closed-source commercial EDA tools for industrial applications. Through these workflows, we assess agents' capabilities in RTL code generation, iterative repair, tool-feedback utilization, logic synthesis, placement and routing (P&R), and Engineering Change Order (ECO) automation. To further characterize the efficiency of agent systems, we introduce Token ROI, a cost-efficiency metric that measures effective improvements in EDA artifacts relative to token usage and runtime cost. Experimental results show that, even when built on the same foundation model, different agent system architectures can exhibit performance gaps of up to 86.27%. Moreover, among systems with comparable task performance, Token ROI can differ by as much as $105.92\times$. In the RTL-to-GDS flow using PicoRV32 as a case study, FluxEDA achieves an end-to-end score of up to 97.94, outperforming Claude Code equipped with domain-specific EDA skills by up to $8.39\times$. These results indicate that domain-specific skills alone are insufficient to improve agent performance in large-scale EDA scenarios. Instead, both agent system design and foundation model capability play critical roles in enabling effective automated EDA workflows.

### [90] [Retain or Consolidate? Budget-Dependent Operator Selection for Language Agent Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17545)
*Qingcan Kang,Mingyang Liu,Shixiong Kai,Kaichao Liang,Zhentao Tang,Yuqi Cui,Tao Zhong,Mingxuan Yuan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 语言agent记忆操作选择，预算依赖，直接涉及记忆管理

TL;DR: 提出了一种预算依赖的记忆整合与保留决策框架，通过分解操作效用并训练轻量级模型OAS来动态选择最优策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆策略（保留和整合）各有优劣，缺乏何时使用哪种以及选择哪个操作符（合并、抽象、重写）的决策准则，且该决策受预算压力影响。

Method: 将每个操作符的效用分解为覆盖效应和替换效应，分析其平衡随预算的变化；训练轻量级模型OAS，利用预生成特征和离线伤害校准估计效用。

Result: 在LongMemEval上，紧张预算下整合提升准确率高达48%，宽松预算下保留更优；LoCoMo上类似交叉。跨笔记抽象和合并优于局部重写。

Conclusion: 记忆策略选择应动态依据预算压力，OAS模型可有效估计效用并指导策略切换。

中文摘要：语言代理依赖于跨交互的记忆。然而，大型语言模型（LLM）有限的上下文窗口及其推理成本限制了每次可使用的记忆量。现有系统主要遵循两种策略：记忆保留和记忆整合。保留策略保持原始记录并保留精确细节，但在预算紧张时相关证据可能无法容纳；整合策略压缩并合并记录，提高每个令牌的覆盖率，但可能丢失查询关键细节。两种策略并非普遍适用。这引发了两个核心问题：何时应将整合替代保留，以及应选择哪种操作符——合并、抽象还是重写？我们通过将每个操作符的效用分解为对保留遗漏证据的覆盖效应和对已适应原始证据的有符号替代效应来形式化这一决策。它们的平衡解释了为何首选行动随相对预算压力而变化。我们通过离线抽象-安全（OAS）实现这一机制，这是一个轻量级学习器，利用预生成特征和保留的伤害校准来估计行动效用。公共LongMemEval和LoCoMo基准测试显示了相同的预算依赖模式。在LongMemEval上，在紧张预算下整合可将绝对准确率提高高达48%，而在宽松预算下保留更优；LoCoMo在较小预算下复制了这种交叉，与其更短的证据一致。在两个数据集上，当需要压缩时，跨笔记抽象和合并通常优于局部重写。

Original abstract: Language agents depend on memory across interactions. However, the limited context windows of large language models (LLMs) and their inference costs constrain how much memory can be used at once. Existing systems mainly follow two strategies: memory retention and memory consolidation. Retention keeps raw records and preserves exact details, but relevant evidence may not fit under a tight budget; consolidation compresses and combines records, improving coverage per token but risking the loss of query-critical details. Neither strategy is universally preferable. This raises two central questions: when should consolidation replace retention, and which operator -- Merge, Abstract, or Rewrite -- should be selected? We formalize this decision by decomposing each operator's utility into a coverage effect on evidence omitted by retention and a signed replacement effect on raw evidence that already fits. Their balance explains why the preferred action changes with relative budget pressure. We implement this mechanism with Offline Abstraction-Safety (OAS), a lightweight learner that estimates action utilities from pre-generation features with held-out harm calibration. The public LongMemEval and LoCoMo benchmarks show the same budget-dependent pattern. On LongMemEval, consolidation improves absolute accuracy by up to 48% under tight budgets, whereas retention is preferable under loose budgets; LoCoMo replicates this crossover at a smaller budget, consistent with its shorter evidence. On both datasets, cross-note abstraction and merging generally outperform local rewriting when compression is necessary.

### [91] [Why Does Feedback-Augmented Self-Distillation Fail to Improve Retrieval-Interleaved Search Agents?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17558)
*Fan Yang,Rui Meng,Yuxin Wen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 检索式搜索agent自蒸馏失败分析，涉及训练与一致性

TL;DR: 提出反馈增强自蒸馏（FA-SD）用于智能体任务，发现解码崩溃现象，并引入EMA教师稳定训练，最终提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索基于策略的自蒸馏在复杂智能体任务中的有效性，并解决因监督信号不一致导致的学习不稳定性问题。

Method: 实例化FA-SD算法，利用成功示范作为特权信息；引入指数移动平均（EMA）教师来缓解自教师模型中的模型不一致和提示不一致。

Result: EMA教师通过提供更稳定的监督信号，尽管需要预热阶段，最终提升了模型在智能体任务上的性能。

Conclusion: 反馈增强自蒸馏结合EMA教师能有效提升大型语言模型在复杂智能体任务上的表现，但需要注意预热阶段可能带来的性能暂时下降。

中文摘要：基于策略的自蒸馏（OPSD）为训练大型语言模型提供了一种有前景的方法，无需依赖单独的教师模型。然而，其在复杂智能体任务上的有效性仍未得到充分探索。在这项工作中，我们实例化了反馈增强自蒸馏（FA-SD），这是一种针对智能体搜索的自蒸馏算法，利用成功的示范作为特权信息。我们发现模型可能依赖重复出现的推理和搜索输出模板，产生看似多样但与输入问题基本无关的轨迹，这使得基于KL散度的自蒸馏信号变得无信息量。我们将这种现象称为解码崩溃，这是一种可能被现有评估指标遗漏的失败模式。为理解其根本原因，我们表明尽管自教师模型取得了更强的性能，但由于监督信号不一致，学习本质上仍然不稳定。我们进一步将这种不一致性分解为模型不一致和提示不一致，并表明后者会显著降低监督信号的质量，限制自教师学习的有效性。为缓解这种不一致性，我们引入指数移动平均（EMA）教师来稳定自教师模型，并提供更一致的监督信号。尽管EMA教师需要一个预热阶段，在此期间性能可能暂时下降，但它通过提供更稳定的监督最终提升了模型性能。

Original abstract: On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) offers a promising approach for training large language models without relying on a separate teacher model. However, its effectiveness on complex agentic tasks remains largely unexplored. In this work, we instantiate Feedback-Augmented Self-Distillation (FA-SD), a self-distillation algorithm for agentic search that leverages successful demonstrations as privileged information. We identify that models can rely on recurring reasoning-and-search output templates, producing trajectories that appear diverse but are largely agnostic to the input question, making the KL-based self-distillation signal uninformative. We term this phenomenon decoding collapse, a failure mode that can be missed by existing evaluation metrics. To understand its underlying cause, we show that although the self-teacher achieves stronger performance, learning remains inherently unstable due to inconsistent supervision signals. We further decompose this inconsistency into model inconsistency and prompt inconsistency, and show that the latter can significantly degrade the quality of the supervision signal, limiting the effectiveness of self-teacher learning. To mitigate this inconsistency, we introduce an exponential moving average (EMA) teacher to stabilize the self-teacher and provide more consistent supervision signals. Although the EMA teacher requires a warm-up phase during which performance may temporarily regress, it ultimately improves model performance by providing more stable supervision.

</details>


### [92] [ZifaMem: Structured Memory for Persona, Preference, and Emotional Continuity in AI Companions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17564)
*Jingzhe Fang,Guozhi Xu,Yunfan Cui,Xiaochen Yang,Zhangyu Hua*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 结构化记忆系统，通用记忆架构可迁移

TL;DR: 提出ZifaMem结构化记忆系统，在多轮对话中提升情感连贯性，相比原始对话历史提高11.4%情感智能分数，与Mem0性能相当。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI伴侣需要情感连贯性，而现有系统仅依赖原始对话历史，缺乏长期记忆和用户模型。

Method: 设计ZifaMem系统，包含会话摘要、情景记忆和整合用户模型，并与原始历史、Mem0等比较，使用LLM评判协议评估。

Result: 结构化记忆提高情感智能11.4%，角色接地提升显著（Claude +42%），多轮情感上下文偏好+39%，额外情感状态机无增益。

Conclusion: 结构化记忆系统显著优于原始历史，ZifaMem与Mem0性能统计等价，开源代码可供使用。

中文摘要：AI伴侣的评判不仅基于单轮流畅性，还取决于它们是否维持情感连续性：记住伴侣是谁、用户偏好什么以及关系感受如何。我们提出ZifaMem，一种结构化记忆系统，将对话组织成会话摘要、情景记忆和整合的用户模型。与提供完整原始对话历史的部署诚实比较器相比，在带有路由审计的固定LLM作为评判者协议下，结构化记忆将池化的四个主干情感智能分数提高了11.4%（95% CI 6.3%至17.1%），且角色接地在所有四个主干上均有改进（Claude相对提高42%）。多轮情感上下文比单轮快照赢得+39%的净偏好（探索性），而额外的情感状态机在五个终结点上均未带来可衡量的收益。在相同的预注册协议下，三种记忆系统（ZifaMem、Mem0和过滤逐字检索）均显著优于原始历史部署，且ZifaMem和Mem0在预注册的主要偏好终结点上统计上等价（差异在±5分以内）。ZifaMem SDK、CLI和可移植Agent Skills已在https://github.com/zifacorp/zifamem开源。

Original abstract: AI companions are judged not only by single-turn fluency but by whether they sustain emotional continuity: remembering who the companion is, what the user prefers, and how the relationship has felt. We present ZifaMem, a structured memory system that organizes dialogue into session summaries, episodic memories, and a consolidated user model. Against a deployment-honest comparator that supplies the full raw dialogue history, and under a fixed LLM-as-a-judge protocol with route audits, structured memory raises pooled four-backbone emotional-intelligence scores by 11.4% (95% CI 6.3% to 17.1%), and persona grounding improves on all four backbones (Claude +42% relative). Multi-turn affect context wins a +39% net preference over a single-turn snapshot (exploratory), whereas an additional emotion state machine yields no measurable gain on any of five endpoints. Under an identical preregistered protocol, three memory systems (ZifaMem, Mem0, and filtered verbatim retrieval) each improve significantly over raw-history deployment, and ZifaMem and Mem0 are statistically equivalent within +/-5 points on the preregistered primary preference endpoint. The ZifaMem SDK, CLI, and portable Agent Skills are open-sourced at https://github.com/zifacorp/zifamem.

</details>


### [93] [A Dual-Hypothesis Reasoning Framework for LLM Guardrails](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17575)
*Md Asiful Islam,Mihai Surdeanu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 双假设推理护栏，可增强agent安全控制

TL;DR: ARBITER是一种LLM护栏框架，通过双假设推理和多组件监督微调，以低成本实现高性能的安全审核，并提供可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于推理的护栏依赖昂贵流程（如使用大型教师模型和全参数微调），缺乏可解释性，且性能有限。

Method: 提出双假设推理方法显式考虑安全与不安全解释，以及多组件监督微调（MC-SFT）分解输出并加权。采用自生成策略和LoRA微调降低开销。

Result: 在三个安全基准上优于现有基线，尤其在域外评估中表现更佳。

Conclusion: ARBITER以低成本实现高性能、可解释的护栏，展示了推理与微调创新的有效性。

中文摘要：我们提出了ARBITER，一种新颖的LLM护栏框架，它引入了两个关键思想：（i）双假设推理，一种用于LLM护栏的推理方法，在做出安全决策之前显式考虑提示的安全和不安全解释；（ii）多组件监督微调（MC-SFT），一种基于推理的护栏的结构化训练损失，将LLM输出分解为逻辑组件并根据其重要性进行加权。现有的基于推理的护栏通常依赖于昂贵的流程，例如使用更大的或闭源的教师模型生成推理轨迹，以及应用全参数微调。相比之下，ARBITER采用经济高效的自生成策略生成推理轨迹，并基于LoRA的参数高效微调，同时仍然实现了比这些昂贵方法更优的性能。此外，ARBITER为不安全决策提供了忠实的证据短语解释，实现了更透明和可解释的护栏方法。在三个安全审核基准上的实验表明，ARBITER优于现有的基于推理和非推理的护栏基线，在域外评估中具有明显的优势。

Original abstract: We propose ARBITER, a novel LLM guardrail framework that introduces two key ideas: (i) dual-hypothesis reasoning, a reasoning method for LLM guardrails that explicitly considers both safe and unsafe interpretations of a prompt before making a safety decision, and (ii) multi-component supervised fine-tuning (MC-SFT), a structured training loss for reasoning-based guardrails that decomposes LLM outputs into logical components and weights them according to their importance. Existing reasoning-based guardrails often rely on expensive procedures, such as generating reasoning traces using larger or closed-source teacher models and applying full-parameter fine-tuning. In contrast, ARBITER uses a cost-effective self-generation strategy for reasoning traces and LoRA-based parameter-efficient fine-tuning while still achieving better performance than these expensive approaches. Additionally, ARBITER provides faithful evidence-phrase explanations for unsafe decisions, enabling a more transparent and interpretable guardrail method. Experiments on three safety moderation benchmarks show that ARBITER outperforms existing reasoning-based and non-reasoning guardrail baselines, with clear gains in out-of-domain evaluations.
